Chapter 0: Introduction & Key Terms (Ch 1)

導論與關鍵術語 | p1-p20

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Technology Transfer (3rd Edition) | p1–p20

本章學習目標

  • 理解 ICH Q10 對技術移轉（Technology Transfer，技術移轉）的官方定義，以及其本質是知識管理而非單純複製製程
  • 掌握技術移轉的三大策略驅動因素：產品生命週期推進、產能擴充/風險分散、策略性業務搬遷
  • 區分 Sending Unit（送出單位）與 Receiving Unit（接收單位）的角色與知識不對稱性，以及如何管理組織關係
  • 辨別 Technology Transfer Charter（技術移轉章程）與 Technology Transfer Proposal（技術移轉提案）的定義差異與使用時機
  • 了解本指南的適用範圍：涵蓋分析方法、原料藥（DS）及藥品（DP）的各類移轉情境，以及本指南不涵蓋的項目

1.1 Background and Purpose｜背景與目的

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p7

Transfer of manufacturing processes and analytical procedures between facilities or laboratories is a necessary part of pharmaceutical development and commercialization. Technology transfers may utilize the outputs of process and method development activities and/or documentation of established processes and methods. Knowledge of the product and the manufacturing process is the basis for transfer to a different location (which could be a different site, country, or facility on the same site) where a process or analytical procedure will be operated.

This Guide focuses on how technology transfer can be achieved.

Technology transfer is defined in ICH Q10 paragraph 3.1.2 as follows:

"The goal of technology transfer activities is to transfer product and process knowledge between development and manufacturing, and within or between manufacturing sites to achieve product realisation. This knowledge forms the basis for the manufacturing process, control strategy, process validation approach and ongoing continual improvement."

Technology transfer projects may take place at various points during the product lifecycle. Successful transfers depend on robust project management processes combined with appropriate product and process understanding. They require partnership, cooperation, and coordination between the sending and receiving units to ensure successful and efficient completion, such that the receiving unit can manufacture, test, and release a safe, efficacious, and quality product comparable to that of the sending unit.

Technology transfer projects are dependent on the development and characterization of robust processes that allow consistent and predictable operation of these processes. Similarly, development of robust analytical methods enables timely transfer of methods. These are particularly important aspects; if processes are not well developed and sources of variation are not well known, e.g., due to incomplete or inadequate process/product knowledge, then technology transfer will not be robust.

This Guide has been designed to present industry good practices for successful and efficient execution of technology transfer projects and to achieve a balance between risk management and cost effectiveness while aligning with applicable regulatory expectations, as described in ICH Q7, Q8(R2), Q9, Q10, and Q11 and other regulatory documents.

The impetus for technology transfer varies and may be based on several factors:

  • Progression in a product development lifecycle, from development through scale-up to commercialization
  • The need for additional manufacturing capacity driven by increased demand or risk mitigation
  • The need to streamline capacity when volumes fall, e.g., at patent expiry, when products change commercial status from novel to generic, etc.
  • Strategic requirements to relocate business units, e.g., regional economic advantages, regional requirements for local manufacture, global expansion in different regions of the world, etc.
  • Identification and qualification of local analytical facilities for testing of intermediates and finished products to meet regional regulatory requirements
  • Dual sourcing strategies to mitigate demand variability or to reduce sourcing risks from manufacturing sites
  • Ensuring adequate turnaround times for analytical laboratories
  • Utilization of virtual organizational structures and increasing use of third parties

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 技術移轉的本質

Technology Transfer（技術移轉）：不是「複製一個製程」，而是將產品與製程知識系統性地遷移，使接收方能獨立製造出與送出方同等品質的產品。

ICH Q10 的定義點出了一個關鍵：TT 的目標是 product realisation（產品實現）。這意味著最終成果是患者拿到一個安全有效的藥物，不只是完成一份文件移交。

三個核心要素：

  • 知識（Knowledge）：包含製程參數、分析方法、CQAs、CPPs 及隱性操作知識
  • 夥伴關係（Partnership）：送出方與接收方必須真正合作，而非單向交付
  • 製程穩健性（Process Robustness）：不穩健的製程無法被成功移轉

比喻說明 — 搬家 vs. 複製一家餐廳

一般人以為技術移轉像「搬家」— 把設備、文件打包，換個地方重新開張。

實際上，更像是讓一位主廚在不同城市複製一家米其林餐廳：食譜（SOP）固然重要，但主廚的手感、食材供應商的品質、廚房設備的微差異、當地員工的習慣——這些「隱性知識」才是決定成敗的關鍵。

技術移轉失敗的根本原因，往往不是設備不符，而是這些「說不清楚的知識」沒有被完整傳遞。

重點提示 — 三大策略驅動因素的風險差異

本指南列出的 TT 動機可歸納為三類，每類有截然不同的風險樣貌：

  • 生命週期推進（Dev→Commercial）：產品知識仍在發展中，最大風險是製程未充分表徵就倉促移轉
  • 產能擴充/風險分散：製程已驗證，風險在於跨廠設備差異與 scale-up
  • 策略性業務搬遷：政治、組織、文化因素主導，技術反而不是最大障礙

身為 CDMO 的接收方，必須在簽約前先判斷：這是哪一類移轉？每類需要的保護機制完全不同。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. ICH Q10 定義中「product realisation」這個詞，在實務上代表哪些具體可交付成果（deliverables）？
  2. 假設你是 CDMO 接收方，送出方告訴你「製程很穩定，直接移轉沒問題」——你應該要求看哪些文件來驗證這個說法？
  3. 「dual sourcing strategy（雙源策略）」對 CDMO 意味著什麼業務機會與挑戰？
1.2 Rationale for this Third Edition｜第三版更新理由

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p8–p9

The Guide has been updated to ensure alignment with relevant guidance publications and terminology used by industry and regulators. Practical case study examples have been added to this third edition; see Chapter 9 (Appendix 2) and Chapter 10 (Appendix 3).

This third edition highlights the following:

  • Alignment with science and risk-based (Quality by Design (QbD)) principles described in ICH Q8(R2), ICH Q9 Quality Risk Management, ICH Q10 Pharmaceutical Quality System, and ICH Q11, including reference to Quality Target Product Profile (QTPP), Critical Quality Attributes (CQAs), Critical Process Parameters (CPPs), material attributes, design space (where used) and, in particular, control strategy
  • Alignment with the process validation concepts and lifecycle approach as described in:
    • ICH Q10 and Q11
    • FDA Guidance for Industry – Process Validation: General Principles and Practices (January 2011)
    • EMA Guideline on process validation for finished products (November 2016)
    • EU GMP Annex 15 Qualification & Validation and similar PIC/S guidances
    • EMA Guideline on process validation for biotechnology-derived active substances (April 2016)
  • Recognition that knowledge management is a critical component of effective technology transfer. Knowledge includes:
    • Scientific and operational information
    • Product quality attributes (e.g., CQAs and material attributes)
    • Overview of process, including unit operations (CPPs, material attributes, etc.)
    • Control strategy
    • Continuous/continual improvement ideas and plans
    • Tacit knowledge (i.e., knowledge from experience rather than explicit knowledge) and means to communicate this knowledge
    • Health, Safety, and Environment (HSE) requirements
    • Learning points from previous collaborative activities
    • Implications for use of specialist tools and techniques such as Process Analytical Technology (PAT), multivariate data analysis, calibration of models, advanced data analytics, etc.
    • Current understanding of potential risks to product quality
  • Industry developments and potential regulatory impacts:
    • Technology transfers driven by acquisitions
    • Global expansion to developing countries
    • Facility consolidation within a company
    • Clinical to commercial transition within the same or different facilities
    • Supply chain driven events (e.g., economic drivers)
    • Utilization of Contract Manufacturing Organizations (CMOs) and contract development organizations, including virtual organizations
    • Increased utilization of platform and single-use systems
    • Introduction of generics and biosimilars
    • Cost efficiencies, either capital or revenue driven
    • Reduced cycle times
    • Local regulatory requirements
  • Recognition that having a robust quality culture, for both sending and receiving units, is important for ensuring successful technology transfer. This is particularly important where cultures are very different between sending and receiving units, which may be due to internal organizational structures, management styles, country specifics, or just individual approaches; these differences should be recognized early and steps taken to ensure appropriate understanding and alignment during the technology transfer.

Helpful guidance is also given in WHO Technical Report No. 961, Annex 7 and the Japan National Institute of Health Sciences Guideline for Technology Transfer (Draft). The FDA Guidance for Industry – Contract Manufacturing Arrangements for Drugs: Quality Agreement, November 2016 also mentions transfers.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 第三版的三大新增重點

與第二版相比，第三版最重要的三個演進：

  • QbD 整合：將 QTPP → CQAs → CPPs 的邏輯鏈明確納入 TT 框架，不再是「把文件打包移過去」，而是移轉整個科學理解體系
  • 知識管理地位提升：「Tacit knowledge（隱性知識）」首次被明確列入必須移轉的知識類型——這是最難但最重要的部分
  • 案例研究（Appendices 2 & 3）：新增生物製劑與小分子的真實案例，是本版最實用的新增內容

比喻說明 — 隱性知識的挑戰

Tacit knowledge（隱性知識）就像一位老師傅用眼神判斷發酵槽的狀態——他知道「就是感覺不對」，卻說不清楚具體數值。

在 TT 中，這類知識包括：「這個步驟要慢一點加，雖然 SOP 沒寫，但快了就會有問題」、「這個供應商的原料換批次一定要跑一個 qualification」。

把隱性知識轉換成顯性文件（如製程觀察影片、操作者訪談記錄），是 TT 最耗時但最值得的投資。

重點提示 — 品質文化差異是最被低估的風險

指南特別強調「quality culture（品質文化）」差異——這在跨國 CDMO 移轉中尤其關鍵。

常見場景：歐美原廠習慣 risk-based deviation management，而亞洲接收方傾向於零偏差容忍。結果：接收方每次遇到輕微偏差就停線，移轉週期被拉長 3 倍。

解法：在 Charter 階段就明確定義兩方的品質文化差異，並建立共識的 deviation handling protocol。

實務應用 — CDMO 角度看第三版的業務意涵

第三版新增的「CMO utilization」明確被列為技術移轉驅動因素之一，表示 ISPE 正式承認 CDMO 在全球藥品生產鏈中的核心地位。

對 CDMO 而言：

  • Single-use systems 的快速普及，要求 CDMO 同時具備 SUS 和 SS 兩套能力
  • Biosimilar 的增長意味著大量成熟品牌藥的 TT 機會（送出方擁有成熟知識）
  • Virtual organization 的趨勢：委託方沒有自己的工廠，CDMO 既是接收方，也是實際的知識保管者

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 「QbD 整合進 TT」在實務操作中，意味著 Technology Package 必須包含哪些額外文件？
  2. 你的公司要從歐洲原廠接收一個生物製劑製程，如何評估兩者的「品質文化差距」並設計彌合計畫？
1.2.1 ICH Q10 Pharmaceutical Quality System and Technology Transfer

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p10–p11

ICH Q10 illustrates the Pharmaceutical Quality System (PQS), and states:

"The PQS covers the entire lifecycle of a product including pharmaceutical development, technology transfer, commercial manufacturing, and product discontinuation as illustrated by the upper portion of the diagram."

ICH Q10 covers the following topics in relation to technology transfer:

  • Product Lifecycle: The product lifecycle, in relation to technology transfers, includes "New product transfers during Development through Manufacturing" and "Transfers within or between manufacturing and testing sites for marketed products."
  • Knowledge Management: "Product and process knowledge should be managed from development through the commercial life of the product up to and including product discontinuation... Knowledge management is a systematic approach to acquiring, analysing, storing and disseminating information related to products, manufacturing processes and components. Sources of knowledge include prior knowledge; pharmaceutical development studies; technology transfer activities; process validation studies; manufacturing experience; innovation; continual improvement; and change management activities."
  • Management of Change in Product Ownership: "When product ownership changes, (e.g., through acquisitions) management should consider the complexity of this and ensure: (a) The ongoing responsibilities are defined for each company involved; (b) The necessary information is transferred."
  • Application of Process Performance and Product Quality Monitoring System throughout the Product Lifecycle: "Monitoring during scale-up activities can provide a preliminary indication of process performance and the successful integration into manufacturing. Knowledge obtained during transfer and scale up activities can be useful in further developing the control strategy."
  • Application of CAPA System throughout the Product Lifecycle: "CAPA can be used as an effective system for feedback, feedforward and continual improvement."
  • Application of Change Management System throughout the Product Lifecycle: "The change management system should provide management and documentation of adjustments made to the process during technology transfer activities."
  • Application of Management Review throughout the Product Lifecycle: "Aspects of management review should be performed to ensure the developed product and process can be manufactured at commercial scale."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — ICH Q10 的 PQS 生命週期框架

ICH Q10 明確將「技術移轉」列為藥品生命週期的正式組成部分，與「開發、商業生產、產品停產」並列。這意味著 TT 不是一次性事件，而是 PQS 持續運作的一部分。

Knowledge Management（知識管理）在 ICH Q10 的定義包含四個動作：
Acquiring（獲取）→ Analysing（分析）→ Storing（儲存）→ Disseminating（傳播）
技術移轉就是這個知識管理循環在「地點」維度上的延伸。

比喻說明 — 技術移轉是企業的「知識 DNA 複製」

想像一家公司的製程知識是細胞中的 DNA。技術移轉就是細胞分裂——目標是子細胞（接收方）獲得完整且功能正常的 DNA 副本。

如果原 DNA 有缺陷（製程未完整表徵），分裂出的子細胞也會攜帶這個缺陷。這就是為什麼指南一再強調：移轉前必須確保製程的穩健性（process robustness）。

重點提示 — Change Management 在 TT 中的特殊地位

ICH Q10 明確要求在 TT 過程中記錄所有製程調整。這對 CDMO 有重要含義：

  • TT 期間的每個製程修改都必須有正式變更管控文件
  • 不能因為「還在移轉階段」就免除 change control 要求
  • 這些記錄在未來的 regulatory submission 和 PPQ 中將被審查

實務上，TT 期間的 change management log 往往成為驗證報告中最重要的附件之一。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. ICH Q10 提到「product ownership changes（產品所有權變更）」時要確保責任明確——在 CDMO 合約中，這對應到哪些具體條款？
  2. CAPA 在 TT 中的應用：如果 PPQ 批次出現偏差，CAPA 應由送出方還是接收方主導？理由是什麼？
1.2.2 Product Lifecycle｜產品生命週期

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p11–p12

Technology transfer expectations are different during the various phases of the product lifecycle. This Guide addresses the transfer of technology from a sending unit to a receiving unit, which may occur at any time during the lifecycle. This Guide assumes all work performed prior to initiating a transfer phase is adequate for enabling transfer of drug substance and/or drug product processes and analytical methods during the product lifecycle.

Reference to the three stages of the process validation lifecycle described in FDA Guidance for Industry – Process Validation: General Principles and Practices is helpful, particularly Stage 1 (Process Design) which relates to product and process understanding.

The adequacy of product and process understanding is fundamental to successful technology transfer. It starts in design and development and captures knowledge in a development report (e.g., includes initial document review, summaries of experiments, QTPP, CQAs, material attributes, identification of sources of variation, and potential risks to product quality). For generics, historical data on product and process understanding should be documented.

Typically, limited development occurs during the technology transfer phase. Exceptions during transfers can be handled by using risk-based approaches when, for example:

  • There are incomplete characterization or process development
  • Scale-up is needed
  • It is decided to start transfer very early (e.g., due to differing production and development site locations) and to make feasibility batches and carry out development work

Utilization of stage gates is an effective approach to initiating and managing a transfer when development and/or characterization activities are occurring in parallel to the transfer.

Investment in experience in the sending unit with the elements of the process or method being transferred can be used to accelerate transfers. Examples include:

  • Solvent runs: Running the process with process solvents only. Useful to complete definition and test the effectiveness of site specific requirements in procedures, automation, and sampling strategies.
  • Live cell runs (in biological processes): Can elucidate site specific sensitivities to process equipment and utilities by executing cell culture stages and monitoring performance.
  • Simulation activities: Can be used to complete the transfer package and test effectiveness without requiring either plant or laboratory time. Often termed table tops, make-a-batch, simulation runs, virtual batch, or test-a-batch.
  • Engineering runs: Executed prior to the initiation of process validation and typically without full GMP controls. Valuable to obtain experience with processes which have significant differences from the sending unit knowledge base, e.g., changes in scale and equipment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — Stage Gates（階段關卡）機制

Stage Gates（階段關卡）是專案管理工具：在 TT 的每個里程碑設置「必須達成條件」，未達成則不能進入下一階段。

典型的 TT Stage Gates：

  • Gate 1：Technology Package 完整性確認 → 才能開始 RU 的場地準備
  • Gate 2：設備/設施 Qualification 完成 → 才能執行工程批
  • Gate 3：工程批結果符合接受標準 → 才能啟動 PPQ
  • Gate 4：PPQ 成功 → 才能正式商業放行

Stage gates 讓「並行開發與移轉」成為可控的風險，而不是失控的混亂。

公式與計算 — 四種加速移轉的技術手段比較

手段            GMP 要求    成本    加速效果    適用情境
──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
Solvent runs    低          低      中          化學合成製程定義
Live cell runs  中          中      高          生物製程設備敏感性
Simulation      無          低      中          文件完整性驗證
Engineering     低          高      最高        scale-up 或設備差異大

CDMO 建議：優先使用 simulation（成本最低），再視差異程度決定是否需要 engineering runs。

重點提示 — 移轉期間「限制開發」的黃金規則

「Typically, limited development occurs during the technology transfer phase」—— 這句話是 TT 最容易被違反的原則。

常見失敗情境：移轉開始後，送出方說「順便優化一下配方」，導致：接收方沒有已驗證的 baseline 可比較、後續 comparability study 無法証明等同性。

規則：移轉期間的製程必須凍結（freeze），任何優化必須通過正式 change control，並重新評估移轉計畫。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的接收方在工程批期間發現一個送出方 SOP 中未描述的關鍵操作步驟。這應觸發什麼程序？由誰負責更新文件？
  2. Stage 1 (Process Design) 的成果如何具體體現在 TT 的 Technology Package 中？
1.2.3 Intellectual Property and Confidentiality | 1.2.4 Quality Agreements

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p12–p13

1.2.3 Intellectual Property and Confidentiality Agreements

Sending and receiving units would normally agree at an early stage what intellectual property can be shared between them or with third parties. From a commercial viewpoint, this is an important fundamental agreement that needs to be implemented early on before a transfer can be organized or its scope quantified. Intellectual property agreements and related confidentiality agreements are typically company and product specific.

1.2.4 Quality Agreements

A quality agreement is required when using a contract partner. It should be a separate document and includes the following aspects:

  • Data integrity
  • Data management and responsibility
  • Information technology requirements
  • Continued Process Verification and its reporting
  • Any continual improvement initiatives
FDA Guidance defines a quality agreement as:

"A quality agreement is a comprehensive written agreement between parties involved in the contract manufacturing of drugs that defines and establishes each party's manufacturing activities in terms of how each will comply with CGMP."

The FDA guidance states that quality agreements should cover manufacturing activities and change control associated with these activities. Manufacturing activities include quality unit activities, facilities and equipment, materials management, product specific considerations, laboratory controls, and documentation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — IP 協議 vs. 品質協議

這兩個協議的功能不同，但必須在 TT 開始前同步到位：

IP / NDA（保密協議）：決定「哪些知識可以共享、共享到什麼程度」，這直接影響 Technology Package 的完整性。IP 協議簽好前，送出方不會揭露核心配方或製程機密。

Quality Agreement（品質協議）：定義「誰對品質負責」，特別是 CGMP 合規義務的分配。根據 FDA 2016 年指南，品質協議是 CDMO 合作的法律前提。

重點提示 — CDMO 接收方的 5 大合約陷阱

在簽 TT 協議前，接收方必須確認：

  1. IP 所有權：移轉過程中 CDMO 優化的製程，IP 歸誰？
  2. Data integrity 責任：誰負責確保電子數據的完整性？
  3. Change control 主導權：送出方若要修改規格，CDMO 是否有否決權？
  4. CPV 報告責任：商業生產後的 Continued Process Verification 由誰執行？
  5. Deviation 處理：CDMO 發現製程問題，通報時限和調查主導方的規定

比喻說明 — 品質協議是「婚前協議」

品質協議就像商業合作的婚前協議（prenuptial agreement）：在關係最好、最願意合作的時候，把未來可能的爭議都寫清楚。

很多 TT 失敗，不是因為技術問題，而是發生問題後雙方在「責任歸屬」上拉鋸，浪費了寶貴的修正時間。品質協議的作用就是讓「誰做什麼、誰負責什麼」在一開始就明確無爭議。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的 CDMO 在 TT 期間發現一個優化機會，可以將 yield 提升 15%。在沒有明確 IP 協議的情況下，你應該如何處理這個發現？
  2. 品質協議中「data management and responsibility」對電子批次記錄（eBR）系統有哪些具體要求？
1.2.5 Science and Risk-Based Approaches and Control Strategy｜科學與風險方法及管控策略

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p13–p15

Technology transfer can be considered to have these main components:

  • Business strategy
  • Regulatory strategy
  • Understanding and agreement of the knowledge to be transferred
  • Understanding of the control strategy to be transferred
  • Robust project management (including accounting for differences in culture and styles of working)

Using science and risk-based (or QbD) approaches enable understanding about a product and its process and the link to patient requirements, and hence enable effective technology transfer. For legacy products, historical information should be captured and documented, including agreed acceptance criteria and ranges within which product quality has been achieved.

Technology transfer should ensure knowledge of product, process, and operational aspects are transferred effectively between sending and receiving units and that risks and mitigation plans during each of the phases are understood. QTPP, CQAs, CPPs, material attributes, and control strategy, as described in ICH Q8(R2), are elements to product and process understanding and should be available during technology transfer.

An effective control strategy includes:

  • Understanding the relationship between CQAs, CPPs, material attributes, and in-process controls
  • Controls on material attributes (including raw materials, starting materials, intermediates, reagents, primary packaging materials for the drug substance, etc.)
  • Controls implicit in the design of the manufacturing process (e.g., sequence of purification steps or order of addition of reagents)
  • In-process controls (including in-process tests and control of process parameters)
  • Controls on drug substance
  • Understanding of analytical methods
  • Having appropriate data
  • Alarm strategies
  • Completed and qualified engineering modifications for equipment or utilities
  • Where applicable, PAT systems, closed loop controls, and validated PAT methods and models

Undertaking small scale batch observation runs can offer benefits (particularly when a CMO is being used):

  • Helps to get support and agreement from production teams
  • Improve knowledge of the process, reduce errors, and build bill of materials lists
  • Allows for the receiving unit team to view these at the sending unit's site and, for example, to make video recordings as appropriate

Ensuring operators understand what has to be implemented is important; some companies include a qualification and training program as part of operator training. Technical groups should explain to operators why the CPPs and controls have specific ranges and, in particular, those which will have a negative impact if out of range.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — Control Strategy（管控策略）的完整定義

ICH Q10 定義：Control Strategy 是「從當前產品和製程理解中衍生的一套計畫性管控措施，確保製程性能和產品品質」。

Control Strategy 的七個層次（從源頭到終點）：

  1. 原料/起始物料的屬性管控
  2. 製程設計隱含的管控（如加料順序）
  3. In-process controls（製程中管控）
  4. 中間體規格
  5. 成品規格
  6. 警報策略（Alarm strategies）
  7. PAT 及閉迴路管控（進階）

移轉 Control Strategy 意味著上述七個層次全部必須在接收方重新建立並驗證。

比喻說明 — Control Strategy 是飛機的自動駕駛系統

製程就像飛機，Control Strategy 就是自動駕駛系統——當某個參數偏移時，系統知道要如何修正，也知道超過哪個邊界就必須報警並由人工介入。

技術移轉「搬」的不只是飛機硬體（設備），而是整個自動駕駛的邏輯（為什麼這個參數要設在這個範圍、超出去會怎樣）。沒有移轉這套邏輯，飛機到了新基地就沒有人知道怎麼飛。

重點提示 — Batch Observation Run（批次觀察）的 CDMO 實踐

指南特別提到：讓接收方人員到送出方場地觀察生產，包括製作影片記錄。這在 CDMO 接案初期是黃金標準做法：

  • 至少安排 2 位接收方工程師到送出方現場，全程觀察 2-3 批生產
  • 重點觀察：操作者的非正式慣例、設備的特殊操作習慣、關鍵步驟的判斷依據
  • 影片記錄可替代文字描述不到的「手法細節」
  • 觀察完後立即製作「觀察報告」，由送出方確認，成為 Technology Package 的一部分

TT 的五大支柱框架

Business Strategy     ← 為什麼要移轉？商業目標是什麼？
       ↓
Regulatory Strategy   ← 如何維持注冊狀態？需要哪些補充申請？
       ↓
Knowledge Transfer    ← QTPP / CQA / CPP / Material Attr.
       ↓
Control Strategy      ← 如何確保接收方的管控等同送出方？
       ↓
Project Management    ← 時程、資源、文化差異管理

這五個支柱缺一不可。最常被忽略的是「Regulatory Strategy」—— 很多 TT 在技術上成功，卻因為沒有提前規劃補充申請而延誤上市。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. CDMO 接收一個「legacy product（傳統產品）」，送出方的製程文件已有 20 年歷史，沒有正式的 QTPP/CQA 文件。你會如何重建 control strategy 的知識基礎？
  2. 批次觀察報告（batch observation report）在後續 PPQ 執行中扮演什麼角色？
1.2.6 Quality Risk Management｜品質風險管理

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p15

Quality Risk Management (QRM), as described in ICH Q9, is an extremely important part of a technology transfer project. Successful technology transfer should ensure all high risk areas have been considered, appropriate mitigation has been put in place, and that any residual risks are assessed and agreed as acceptable between sites. The QRM process should be documented.

The sending and receiving units should follow QRM principles. SOPs related to QRM should be in place and followed in all aspects related to technology transfer.

The terminology, tools, and techniques from ICH Q9 should be used appropriately. Refer to Section 3.3 for additional information. Refer to Chapter 12 (Appendix 5) and Chapter 13 (Appendix 6) for examples of Failure Mode and Effects Analysis (FMEA) and fishbone diagrams.

Risk assessments should ideally be carried out jointly by the sending and receiving units. There should be clear understanding of the purpose of each risk assessment. Any mitigations should be built into control strategies or other procedures at the receiving unit.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — QRM 在 TT 中的三個核心問題

ICH Q9 的 QRM 框架應用於 TT，需要回答三個問題：

  • What can go wrong?（什麼會出錯）：使用 FMEA 或 Fishbone 系統性識別風險
  • What is the likelihood and severity?（可能性與嚴重性）：用風險矩陣量化，聚焦高風險項目
  • What can be done to reduce the risk?（如何降低風險）：設計 mitigation 措施，並建入 control strategy

關鍵要求：風險評估必須由雙方共同執行，不能只是送出方的單方判斷——因為接收方了解自己廠房的特定限制。

重點提示 — Residual Risk（殘餘風險）的管理

不是所有風險都能完全消除。指南要求：殘餘風險必須被雙方明確「評估並接受（assessed and agreed as acceptable）」。

這在實務中意味著：需要正式的 Risk Acceptance 文件，由雙方授權人員簽署，成為 TT 文件包的一部分。這份文件在未來稽核時是保護雙方的重要記錄。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 列舉 3 個 TT 特有的高風險領域（非一般製程驗證風險），並說明如何在 FMEA 中評估它們。
  2. 當送出方的 QRM SOP 與接收方不同時，應如何決定 TT 期間使用哪套方法論？
1.2.7 Communication｜溝通

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p15

The success of technology transfer is critically dependent on good communication and relationships between personnel in technology transfer teams. At the start of a technology transfer, roles and responsibilities should be defined for transfer team members (from both sending and receiving units) including who are responsible and accountable for the components of the transfer.

Sending and receiving units should have the same level of understanding for all aspects of the transfer.

In addition, communication channels and methods (e.g., reports) that may affect the transfer of information should be defined. It is essential that good verbal and written communication channels are put in place, particularly when personnel are often not in the same room and therefore are unable to have face-to-face discussions, e.g., use of teleconferencing and video conferencing. The need to build good relationships and trust between the sending and receiving units is of great importance; capturing and documenting all appropriate knowledge is crucial so that it can be easily communicated between the sending and receiving units.

For transfers between companies, communication should be formalized by leveraging documents such as quality and supply agreements. A similar formality in principle should be put in place for intra-company transfers.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

重點提示 — 溝通是 TT 成敗的隱藏變數

指南使用了「critically dependent（關鍵依賴）」這個措辭來描述溝通的重要性——這是全章最強烈的措辭之一。

TT 失敗案例分析顯示：超過 60% 的問題根源可追溯到溝通不良，而非技術缺陷。常見的溝通失敗模式：

  • 送出方認為「已在文件中說明」，接收方認為「文件太模糊」
  • 問題在非正式場合口頭解決，但沒有文字記錄
  • 跨時區、跨語言導致的資訊衰減（information decay）
  • 「不敢問」的文化障礙——接收方不好意思承認沒看懂

比喻說明 — TT 溝通就像手術室的交班

醫院手術室有嚴格的「Handover（交班）」協議——主刀醫師交班給下一位時，必須按結構化清單逐一確認每個關鍵資訊，不能靠口頭模糊帶過。

TT 的知識交接應該採用同樣的嚴格度：每次溝通後有書面記錄、每個技術決定都有文件追蹤、每個「我們都理解了」都需要雙方確認簽名。

實務應用 — CDMO 溝通架構設計

建議在 Charter 中明確定義的溝通機制：

  • 每週技術例會：固定時間，雙方 PM + 技術負責人，有 minutes
  • 雙週進度報告：標準模板，涵蓋 milestone、open issues、決策記錄
  • 緊急溝通路徑：關鍵偏差 24 小時通報機制，指定單一聯絡窗口
  • 現場訪問計畫：預先排定雙方交叉現場訪問時程，不能靠「有需要再說」

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如何在 TT Charter 中設計一個「溝通有效性評估機制」，確保雙方真正達到相同的理解水準？
  2. 跨公司 TT 中，哪些溝通應該正式化（書面化），哪些可以保持非正式？邊界如何劃定？
1.3 Scope｜適用範圍

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p15–p17

This Guide is intended to be used as a generic guide to technology transfer and compiles information under three main topics:

  • Technology transfer of analytical methods
  • Technology transfer of drug substance (active pharmaceutical ingredients (APIs))
  • Technology transfer of drug product (dosage forms manufacturing processes)

Each topic should be read in conjunction with Chapters 2 and 3 of this Guide. It is recognized that transfers of analytical methods, drug substance, and drug product are closely linked. Drug substance/drug product transfers cannot usually be performed correctly if the corresponding analytical methods are not transferred to validate the transfer for quality.

This Guide is intended to provide information for technology transfers between two parties (a sending unit and a receiving unit) for any applicable transfers in the product lifecycle, e.g.:

  • Laboratory to laboratory scale
  • Laboratory to development/pilot scale
  • Development to clinical manufacturing
  • Development to launch/commercial manufacturing
  • Commercial to commercial manufacturing
  • Drug substance to drug product manufacture
  • Lead manufacturer to third party manufacturer

The sending and receiving units may be internal (within the same company) or external (between companies or to a third party such as a CMO). The transfer is normally from a sending unit that possesses the process knowledge, history, and operational experience to a receiving unit which needs to acquire that knowledge and leverage available experience to manufacture the drug.

This Guide makes reference to, but does not cover, the following aspects:

  • Regulatory guidance
  • Qualification and process validation
  • Product and process development

The topics of Continued Process Verification (CPV) and Continued Quality Verification (CQV) are beyond the scope of this Guide. A technology transfer is considered complete after the close-out phase.

However, process validation is an important step to ensure technology transfer has been completed and the links are summarized in Table 1.1 in simple terms.

Process Validation Stages Nomenclature (US) Technology Transfer Links to Process Validation
1 Process Design Technology transfer requires an understanding of what has to be transferred, e.g., CQAs, CPPs, material attributes, and control strategy.
2.1 Qualification of Utilities and Equipment Utilities and equipment at the receiving unit (especially if it is different between sending and receiving units) is confirmed to operate over the ranges for the CPPs required.
2.2 Process Performance Qualification (PPQ) Confirms the receiving unit can deliver the CQAs.
3 Continued Process Verification (CPV) Ensures the receiving unit puts in place monitoring to ensure technology transfer has been successfully delivered.

Table 1.1: Technology Transfer Links to Process Validation

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 範圍的三個維度

本指南的範圍可從三個維度理解：

技術類型維度：分析方法 + DS + DP，三者必須同步移轉——沒有分析方法的移轉，無法驗證 DS/DP 的品質等同性。

生命週期維度：從 lab-to-lab 到 commercial-to-commercial，7 種移轉情境全部涵蓋。CDMO 最常處理的是後三種（Dev→Commercial、Commercial→Commercial、Lead→Third Party）。

組織維度：內部移轉（intra-company）與外部移轉（inter-company/CDMO）。指南對兩者的要求在原則上相同，但外部移轉多了 IP、質量協議等層面。

重點提示 — TT 與 Process Validation 的邊界

指南明確說明 TT 在「close-out phase（結案階段）」之後即完成，CPV 和 CQV 不在本指南範圍內。但 Table 1.1 清楚顯示 TT 與 Process Validation 的深度連結：

  • Stage 1 (Process Design) = TT 的「知識輸入」來源
  • Stage 2.1 (Equip/Utility Q) = TT 「接收方準備」的核心工作
  • Stage 2.2 (PPQ) = TT 成功的「終極驗證」
  • Stage 3 (CPV) = TT 之後的持續監控（超出本指南）

實務上，TT 計畫與 Process Validation Plan 應該從一開始就整合撰寫，避免重複或矛盾。

比喻說明 — 三類移轉的不同挑戰

Dev→Commercial：像把大學實驗室的配方交給食品工廠量產——尺度、設備、員工技能都完全不同，最大挑戰是 scale-up 和製程穩健性。

Commercial→Commercial（同公司）：像連鎖餐廳把菜單從台北店複製到高雄店——核心挑戰是地區差異（水質、供應商、員工習慣）的管理。

Lead→Third Party（CDMO）：像把廚師連同配方都租給別人的餐廳——IP 保護、品質文化對齊、長期合約關係才是核心挑戰。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. Table 1.1 中，PPQ 的成功是否等同於 TT 的成功？兩者有哪些可能的差距？
  2. 一個 CDMO 同時承接「analytical method TT」和「DP process TT」，兩者的時程應如何協調？哪個必須先完成？
1.4 Key Terms｜關鍵術語

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Tech Transfer 3rd Ed. | p17–p18

This section introduces key terms as they are used in the context of this Guide. Refer to Chapter 15 for an expanded listing of definitions.

Control Strategy

As defined in ICH Q10:
"A planned set of controls, derived from current product and process understanding, that assures process performance and product quality. The controls can include parameters and attributes related to drug substance and drug product materials and components, facility and equipment operating conditions, in-process controls, finished product specifications, and the associated methods and frequency of monitoring and control."

Receiving Unit

An organization, which includes core and auxiliary functions, where a designated product, process, or method is expected to be transferred to.

Core functions normally include quality, manufacturing, and process engineering. Auxiliary functions may include regulatory, supply chain, warehousing, and HSE. The actual balance of functions would be project specific.

Process Validation

As defined in FDA Guidance for Industry – Process Validation: General Principles and Practices:

"Collection and evaluation of data, from the process design stage through commercial production, which establishes scientific evidence that a process is capable of consistently delivering quality product."

Note: This is a lifecycle definition covering the three stages as described by FDA.

As defined in EMA Guideline on process validation for finished products:

"Documented evidence that the process, operated within established parameters, can perform effectively and reproducibly to produce a medicinal product meeting its predetermined specifications and quality attributes."

Note: This definition refers to a single stage – equivalent to Stage 2.2 of FDA Guidance.

Quality Target Product Profile (QTPP)

As defined in ICH Q8(R2):
"A prospective summary of the quality characteristics of a drug product that ideally will be achieved to ensure the desired quality, taking into account safety and efficacy of the drug product."

Sending Unit

An organization, which includes core and auxiliary functions, where a designated product, process, or method is expected to be transferred from.

Core functions normally include quality, manufacturing, and process engineering. Auxiliary functions may include regulatory, supply chain, warehousing, and HSE.

Stakeholder

Any individual, group, or organization that can affect, be affected by, or perceive itself to be affected by a transfer. Decision makers might also be stakeholders.

Technology Transfer Charter

The technology transfer charter captures the strategic intent and defines the overall scope of the technology transfer project. It should document the team members and their roles and responsibilities, explain the effort and time required for the technology transfer project, and identify significant assumptions and risks. The charter helps to ensure that management and team members from both sending and receiving units understand the project and agree upon deliverables.

Note: The technology transfer charter and proposal may be the same document, depending on the complexity of the technology transfer project. If the charter elements change, the project needs to be reevaluated, no matter what stage it is at in the technology transfer.

Technology Transfer Proposal

The technology transfer proposal defines the overall scope of the project, documents the team members and their roles and responsibilities, estimates the effort and time required for the project, establishes high level success criteria, and identifies significant assumptions and risks. This document is intended to ensure that stakeholders and team members from both sending and receiving units understand the project and agree upon the deliverables. The technology transfer proposal also identifies information needed for the technology transfer package. The technology transfer proposal should be reviewed and approved by the appropriate stakeholders from both sending units and receiving units. The proposal may be managed using formal change control procedures.

Note: The technology transfer charter and proposal may be the same document, depending on the complexity of the technology transfer project.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — Charter vs. Proposal：兩份文件的本質差異

指南的 Note 說「兩者可能是同一份文件」——但在複雜的 CDMO 移轉中，它們通常是獨立文件，功能截然不同：

面向 Charter（章程） Proposal（提案）
目的 策略性授權文件 詳細技術計畫
受眾 管理層、決策者 執行團隊、技術人員
內容 目標、範圍、角色、假設 詳細活動、時程、成功標準
核准層級 高層管理授權 專案干係人確認
時機 最先完成 Charter 核准後展開

黃金規則：Charter 確立「做不做、做什麼」；Proposal 確立「怎麼做」。Charter 必須先簽，Proposal 才有正當性。

比喻說明 — Charter 與 Proposal 如同建案許可 vs. 施工圖

Charter 就像建案的「都市計畫許可」——政府（管理層）授權你在這塊地上蓋這類建築（TT 的策略範圍與目標）。

Proposal 就像「施工圖」——建築師（技術團隊）根據許可的範圍，設計出具體的每一道牆要在哪裡、每個管線要怎麼走。

如果一開始建案許可就搞錯了（Charter 定義了錯誤的範圍），再精美的施工圖也是白做——因此指南特別強調：Charter 一旦改變，整個專案必須重新評估。

CDMO 接收方的 5 大必問清單

簽 TT 協議前，接收方必須向送出方確認：

1. 製程表徵完整性
   → 是否有完整的 QTPP/CQA/CPP 矩陣？
   → 哪些 CPP 範圍仍在定義中？

2. Technology Package 的完整性
   → 文件清單是否已確定？隱性知識如何傳遞？
   → 分析方法是否已驗證並可移轉？

3. 法規狀態
   → 現有注冊檔案的狀態？CDMO 接收後需要哪些補充申請？
   → 是否有任何未解決的 regulatory commitment？

4. 設備與設施差異
   → 接收方設備與送出方的關鍵差異？
   → 是否有已知的 scale effect 或設備敏感性？

5. 時程與資源
   → 送出方能提供多少現場支援時間？
   → 關鍵里程碑（first PPQ batch）的目標日期是否現實？

重點提示 — Sending Unit 與 Receiving Unit 的知識不對稱

指南定義顯示：送出方「possesses the process knowledge, history, and operational experience」，接收方「needs to acquire that knowledge」。

這個不對稱性是 TT 中最深層的張力來源：

  • 送出方可能不知道自己知道什麼（隱性知識），無法主動識別出需要移轉的內容
  • 接收方不知道自己不知道什麼，無法問出正確的問題
  • 雙方都可能高估知識移轉的完整性（「我們覺得說清楚了」）

解法：使用結構化的 Technology Package Checklist（見 Appendix 1），強制雙方逐項確認，而非依賴主觀感覺。

重點提示 — FDA vs. EMA 製程驗證定義的差異

指南並列兩個定義，這個差異在 TT 中有實際意義：

  • FDA：生命週期定義（覆蓋 Stage 1-3）— 意味著 PPQ 只是驗證的開始，後續 CPV 同樣重要
  • EMA：單一階段定義（等同 Stage 2.2）— 強調「documented evidence」，PPQ 的批次數據是核心

對於需要同時滿足 FDA 和 EMA 要求的全球產品（常見於 CDMO），TT 的 Process Validation Strategy 必須同時設計兩套邏輯，並在 Regulatory Strategy 中明確說明。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果 Charter 在 TT 進行到一半時需要修改範圍（例如增加一個劑型），正確的程序是什麼？由誰來決定是否需要重新評估整個專案？
  2. QTPP 的定義說「prospective summary（前瞻性摘要）」——這意味著 QTPP 必須在移轉開始前就存在，還是可以在移轉期間建立？對 legacy products 有什麼含義？
  3. 你的 CDMO 是一個複雜 TT 中的「Stakeholder」嗎？Stakeholder 的定義對 CDMO 的參與權有什麼法律意涵？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • TT 的本質是知識管理：ICH Q10 定義明確——技術移轉的目標是「product realisation」，核心是將產品與製程知識從開發端移轉至生產端，而非單純複製設備或 SOP。
  • 送出方與接收方的知識不對稱是 TT 失敗的根源：隱性知識（Tacit knowledge）和品質文化差異往往比技術差距更難克服，必須在 Charter 階段就開始正視。
  • 三大 TT 驅動因素（生命週期推進、產能擴充、策略搬遷）各有不同的風險樣貌，接收方在評估 TT 機會時必須先判斷屬於哪一類。
  • Charter 在 Proposal 之前：Charter 是策略性授權文件（管理層共識），Proposal 是詳細技術計畫（執行團隊指南）——兩者缺一不可，順序不可顛倒。
  • 分析方法移轉是 DS/DP 移轉的前提：沒有已移轉的分析方法，就無法驗證製程的等同性——三類 TT 必須協調規劃，不能獨立推進。
  • TT 與 Process Validation 的邊界：TT 在 close-out 後完成，PPQ 是 TT 成功的終極驗證標誌，CPV 則超出 TT 的範疇——但三者必須在計畫初期就整合設計。
1

Chapter 1: Planning, Success Criteria & TT Phases 1–3 (Ch 2–3a)

規劃、成功標準與技術轉移第1-3階段 | p21-p40

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Technology Transfer (3rd Edition) | p21–p40 ISPE

本章學習目標

  • 理解技術轉移成功標準（Success Criteria）的三個維度：技術、法規、商業，並掌握為何必須在轉移開始前定義這些標準
  • 區分技術轉移章程（Charter）與技術轉移提案（TT Proposal）的功能差異，避免因文件混淆造成範疇蔓延（scope creep）
  • 掌握技術套件（Technology Package）的核心內容，理解哪些知識一旦遺漏將導致轉移失敗
  • 應用品質風險管理（QRM）工具（FMEA、魚骨圖、差距分析）識別技術、法規、組織三類風險
  • 以 CDMO 接收單位視角評估 Phase 1–3 的關鍵交付物與決策節點
Chapter 2 — Technology Transfer: Planning Considerations and Success Criteria｜第二章：技術轉移規劃考量與成功標準
2.1 Introduction｜導論

原文內容 Original Text

This chapter provides guidance on what to consider for a transfer, including establishing success criteria, prior to the formal formation of the full technology transfer team. Guidance provided is applicable to drug substance, drug product, and analytical procedure technology transfers.

A technology transfer typically starts with an agreement (referred to as a charter in Chapter 3) normally formalized or on a contractual basis between a sending unit and a receiving unit for the transfer of, e.g., a developed process or a commercial process or an analytical method.

The success of a technology transfer project will be largely dependent upon the skill and performance of individuals assigned to the project from both the sending unit and the receiving unit. It is, therefore, critical that a clear objective for any technology transfer project be developed. It is also critical that a project team comprised of individuals from both the sending unit and the receiving unit is established and that there is a precise understanding of each team member's role and responsibility prior to initiation of the technology transfer project.

"Skill alone will not ensure a successful technology transfer project. Once a project has been identified and a team chosen, a clear and realistic project implementation plan is required to guide the project, manage expectations, and handle the inevitable deviations and changes that may present themselves during implementation."

Along with that plan comes the need to consider the relationship between the various tasks associated with a successful technology transfer. It should be clearly understood that each technology transfer assignment is unique; therefore, it is impossible to provide a generic technology transfer plan.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Sending Unit（送出單位）：持有製程或分析方法的一方，通常是研發單位、原廠，或另一個生產廠。

Receiving Unit（接收單位）：承接並執行該製程的一方，在 CDMO 情境下，通常就是我們自己。

Success Criteria（成功標準）：技術轉移在「什麼條件下」算成功的預先定義。本章的核心論點是：這些標準必須在轉移開始前定義，而非事後補充。

比喻說明 Analogy

技術轉移就像廚師交接食譜給另一家餐廳。光有食譜不夠——接手的廚師需要知道這道菜的「標準」：顧客吃到什麼味道算成功？廚房設備不同怎麼辦？如果到出餐後才爭論標準，雙方都會痛苦。

重點提示 Key Notes

本指南明確指出，每個技術轉移都是獨一無二的，不存在通用計畫範本。這對 CDMO 特別重要——不能用同一套 SOP 套用所有客戶的轉移案。每個專案都需要客製化的計畫。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼成功標準應在技術轉移「開始前」而非「完成後」定義？若事後才定義會有什麼風險？
  2. 在您目前的 CDMO 操作中，是否有清楚界定送出單位與接收單位各自的責任範圍？
2.2 Technology Transfer Planning Considerations｜技術轉移規劃考量

原文內容 Original Text

In the early planning phase, a charter may not be fully developed yet. In this case, the team should document, at a minimum, the major deliverables and assumptions not expected to change. Examples include:

  • High level program deliverables such as delivery of material to clinical trials or early planning (e.g., for analytical methods)
  • Agency submission strategies
  • Site licensure milestones
  • Budget
  • Mechanism for handling changes, e.g., in scope or budget

As stated earlier, technology transfer can be considered a transfer of knowledge using well founded project management principles.

2.2.1 Developing an Early Agreement Between the Sending and Receiving Units

An agreement (referred to as a charter in Chapter 3) is typically high level and developed with input from sending and receiving unit Subject Matter Experts (SMEs); input is rarely from the full technology transfer team. Securing an early agreement, sometimes referred to as site selection, may be necessary to release the full resources required for detailed planning and execution.

It is increasingly common that early stages with long lead times are initiated prior to formation of the entire team. It is also often necessary to make an early assessment of HSE aspects; an example is a facility that is not capable of handling particular compounds from an HSE standpoint.

By its nature, a technology transfer requires effective management of incomplete information; consideration of information and SME availability is required to determine appropriate planning timelines.

2.2.2 Sending Unit and Receiving Unit Working Closely

Technology transfer planning should be initiated as early as possible. Roles and responsibilities for sending and receiving units should be defined early and updated frequently in the early planning stages. Effective planning and diligent tracking of potential issues can help to expedite technology transfer projects and prevent delays.

A plan created by collaboration between sending and receiving units can help to unify the technology transfer team and to ensure that there is agreement on deliverables, success criteria, and ownership of the transfer at different stages. Project management tools such as the RACI matrix can be useful to formalize roles.

RACI: R = Responsible (實際執行者), A = Accountable (最終責任者), C = Consulted (需徵詢意見者), I = Informed (需告知結果者)

The relationship within the technology transfer team should be actively maintained. Partnership between sending/receiving project managers and accountable functional area leads is key to actively managing the flow of known and emerging process, method, and site capability knowledge.

It is important to understand the critical path timetable and ensure that the technology transfer planning and execution timelines are consistent with the critical path timing. Communicating an unrealistic timeline to management could result in the team's acceptance of undesirable risks in order to meet their commitment.

People to people interaction should be encouraged, especially between counterparts in the sending unit and receiving unit. This is especially important where different cultures exist between sending and receiving units.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

RACI Matrix（責任分配矩陣）：一種專案管理工具，用於釐清每項任務誰負責執行（R）、誰有最終問責（A）、誰需要被諮詢（C）、誰需要被告知（I）。在技術轉移中，送出單位與接收單位各自的 RACI 必須書面化，避免「以為對方會做」的灰色地帶。

Critical Path（關鍵路徑）：專案中影響最終完成日期的最長任務鏈。任何在關鍵路徑上的任務若延誤，整個轉移就會延誤。

比喻說明 Analogy

RACI 矩陣就像餐廳的 HACCP 計畫一樣——每個控制點都要指定「誰量、誰記錄、誰核准、誰被通知」。技術轉移若沒有 RACI，就像廚房裡大家都以為別人會量油溫，最後沒人量。

重點提示 Key Notes

HSE 要早評估：健康、安全、環境（Health, Safety and Environment）的評估必須在計畫初期就完成，因為可能需要長前置期（long lead time）的設施改造或許可申請。CDMO 若接收含毒性化合物或特殊物質的專案，這個評估往往決定是否能承接。

時程務實性：指南特別警告——對管理層報告不切實際的時程，會讓團隊被迫接受不應接受的風險。這在 CDMO 的商業壓力下尤其重要。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在您的 CDMO 最近一次技術轉移中，RACI 矩陣是否有書面化？哪些職責是最容易模糊的？
  2. 「人與人之間的互動」對於不同文化之間的技術轉移為何特別重要？
2.2.3–2.2.4 Roles, Responsibilities & Effective Knowledge Transfer｜角色責任與有效知識移轉

原文內容 Original Text

2.2.3 Clear Understanding of Roles and Responsibilities

A clear understanding of roles and responsibilities for team members, from both the sending and receiving units, serves to minimize redundancies and oversights. Knowing what is expected by other team members can increase accountability and help to minimize confusion and conflicts.

Additional recommendations include:

  • Performing an assessment of the team capabilities relative to the skills required to complete tasks for which team members are accountable
  • Defining decision rights (i.e., who will make the decision regarding particular aspects or differences of view)
  • Defining clear communication routes both within the team and external to the team using, e.g., meetings, shared network or other project sites, meeting minutes
  • Documenting roles and responsibilities with appropriate project management tools such as a RACI matrix

2.2.4 Effective Knowledge Transfer

It is very important that both sending and receiving units discuss and agree the knowledge to be transferred — scientific, regulatory, operational (including tacit knowledge), business, and cultural.

Scientific aspects include:

  • Process description, rationale, history, flow diagrams, unit operations, scale, and material transfers
  • Understanding what is important to control for both drug substance and drug product manufacture (see ICH Q8(R2)) including impact on packaging
  • Ensuring CQAs are understood by both sending and receiving units
  • Analytical technology required to measure process performance (HPLC equipment, columns, etc.)
  • Transferring the control strategies and operationalizing it — note: even for legacy products, regulators are increasingly expecting a QTPP, CQAs and control strategies to be in place
  • Being clear on CPPs and material attributes for each unit operation; design space if used
  • Multivariate approaches (design space, PAT tools, real time release testing, continuous manufacturing)
  • Potential sources of variation

Regulatory aspects include:

  • Compliance with regulatory requirements in both the operating country and the supply country (individual countries may have their own variation guidelines)
  • Some countries require additional bioequivalence studies
  • Validation carried out appropriately including lifecycle approach
  • Adequacy of the QMS/Pharmaceutical Quality System (ICH Q10)
  • Checking no regulatory changes in progress that could impact implementation

Operational aspects (including tacit knowledge) include:

  • Facility and utility requirements; facility fit
  • Operator training and/or qualification requirements
  • Equipment principles that may differ (mixers, dryers using different engineering principles)
  • Developing new manufacturing instructions and SOPs
  • HSE requirements (containment, operator protection)
  • Differences in shifts, automation, PAT tools, scale, batch sizes, process flows, sampling techniques
  • Understanding tacit knowledge — knowledge not explicitly documented but shows actual practices (e.g., scalability, vessel charging, analyst technique)
  • Long term planning for raw materials (import license restrictions)
  • Operators from sending unit working at receiving site (knowledge transfer, visa requirements, QA, HSE concerns)

Business aspects include:

  • Importance of the product being transferred (profitability may differ between units)
  • Determining who pays for what (new equipment, training)
  • Capital responsibility — who invests, who owns the asset, depreciation

Cultural aspects: Gaining understanding of a company or country's culture can significantly contribute to success. Some cultures may be procedural, hierarchical, unstructured, or relationship dependent. Language differences in SOPs and operator communication are also a factor. (Refer to ISPE Cultural Excellence Report [13].)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Tacit Knowledge（默會知識）：指「做得出來但說不清楚」的隱性操作知識。例如，攪拌槳的進料方式、分析師實際如何執行樣品前處理——這些資訊在 SOP 中往往付之闕如。指南明確要求將這類知識文件化，這是技術轉移中最難但最重要的一步。

QTPP / CQA / CPP：
QTPP（Target Product Quality Profile，目標產品品質概況）：最終產品應具備的品質標準
CQA（Critical Quality Attribute，關鍵品質屬性）：直接影響安全性、有效性的品質特性
CPP（Critical Process Parameter，關鍵製程參數）：對 CQA 有顯著影響的製程參數

比喻說明 Analogy

默會知識就像頂級廚師的「手感」——書上寫「攪拌至適當稠度」，但沒人告訴你那個稠度是什麼感覺。技術轉移若只傳遞 SOP 而不傳遞這種手感，接收廚房（CDMO）的第一批產品往往失敗。最好的解法是讓送出單位的廚師親自來廚房示範幾次。

重點提示 Key Notes

五大知識類型：指南將需要轉移的知識分為五類——科學、法規、操作（含默會知識）、商業、文化。CDMO 在接收新案時，往往專注在科學和操作層面，容易忽略法規合規差異（不同國家的送件策略）和文化差異（客戶來自不同管理文化）。

法規層面的隱形地雷：指南特別提醒，legacy product（老產品）的客戶也被監管機構要求提供 QTPP 和 CQA 文件。CDMO 在承接老產品轉移時，若客戶無法提供這些文件，可能需要協助重建，這必須計入報價和時程。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 接收單位在評估新轉移案時，應建立一份標準的知識查核清單，涵蓋以上五類。特別要確認：（1）送出單位是否能提供設計空間文件；（2）分析方法是否使用相同設備平台（HPLC 品牌、管柱型號）；（3）該產品在哪些市場銷售，各市場的法規要求是否一致。這些問題若在商業談判階段就提出，可避免後期巨大的補救成本。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您是否曾在技術轉移後才發現送出單位有重要的「默會知識」未被傳遞？如何在下次避免？
  2. 文化差異如何影響 CDMO 與客戶（送出單位）之間的溝通效率？
2.2.5–2.2.7 Information Package, QRM & Stage Gates｜資訊套件、品質風險管理與階段閘門

原文內容 Original Text

2.2.5 Information Package

A sufficiently complete technology transfer package of information should be developed to meet the requirements of the technology transfer. Refer to Chapter 3, Chapter 8, and Chapter 13 for additional information.

2.2.6 Quality Risk Management

QRM is integral to technology transfer and should follow ICH Q9 principles (see Figure 2.1) or similar. It is important that teams are rigorous in their application of Q9 and spend sufficient time during the initiation phase to ensure full understanding by both sending and receiving units of the purpose of the QRM exercise.

Once the initiation phase is completed, a detailed risk assessment should be carried out (e.g., using tools such as cause and effect matrices, Ishikawa (fishbone) diagrams, gap analysis, and FMEA). After agreement on acceptable and unacceptable risks, then the unacceptable risks should be mitigated to an acceptable level and then controlled through a defined risk mitigation plan.

QRM is an iterative activity. All technology transfer projects require risk assessment. Existing risk assessments may need to be adapted to acknowledge changes in risk during the technology transfer. It is helpful to have a QRM plan if there will be multiple risk assessments. Note that there can be several types of risk assessment — for the project, the process, the product, the equipment, etc. Normally, the project manager would own the project risk assessments and the technical team would own the technical risk assessments.

2.2.7 Phases and Stage Gate Approach

The technology transfer project may be approached in phases (stages). Documentation of the project should include the important activities for each phase, e.g., reviews, deliverables, and projected timelines. Refer to Chapter 3 for the six phases of technology transfer.

Throughout the project, stage gate reviews should be used to ensure that all critical items from the current project phase have been completed satisfactorily before moving on to subsequent phases. This approach helps to ensure critical project items are completed on time and that later phases of technology transfer are not put at risk. Stage gate reviews should be attended by stakeholders and the technology transfer team.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

QRM（Quality Risk Management，品質風險管理）：根據 ICH Q9，QRM 的核心流程包括：風險識別 → 風險分析 → 風險評估 → 風險控制（降低或接受）→ 風險回顧。在技術轉移中，QRM 是識別送出單位與接收單位差異的正式工具。

Stage Gate（階段閘門）：每個階段結束時的正式審查點，確認所有關鍵交付物完成後才放行進入下一階段。這防止「問題堆積到後期才爆發」的常見情況。

QRM 工具比較 QRM Tools

工具              適用場景
FMEA             評估每個失效模式的嚴重性、
（失效模式分析）  發生率、可偵測性（RPN值）

Fishbone Diagram 找出造成問題的根本原因
（魚骨/石川圖）  （人、機、料、法、環）

Gap Analysis     系統性比對送出/接收單位
（差距分析）     的設備、方法、法規要求

Cause-Effect     多因子交互影響的視覺化
Matrix（原因效果矩陣）

重點提示 Key Notes

多層次風險評估：指南提醒，技術轉移中的風險評估不只一種——專案風險（時程、資源）由專案經理負責；製程/產品風險（技術層面）由技術團隊負責。兩者不應混為一談，也不應由同一人獨攬。

Stage Gate 的紀律：台灣很多 CDMO 在專案壓力下往往跳過 stage gate 或「形式審查」。ISPE 明確要求利害關係人（stakeholders）親自出席，說明這是高層決策的審查，不是工程師自己確認就好。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在您的 CDMO 技術轉移流程中，哪個 QRM 工具最常被使用？FMEA 和 Gap Analysis 各自的優勢是什麼？
  2. Stage Gate Review 在您的組織是如何執行的？有哪些常見的「走過場」問題需要改善？
2.3 Technology Transfer Success Criteria｜技術轉移成功標準

原文內容 Original Text

Technology transfer is considered successful if the receiving unit can consistently produce material through the qualified process and demonstrate that quality attributes have been maintained through process monitoring and analysis of the material produced.

"Simply stated, technology transfer can be considered successful if the receiving unit can routinely reproduce the transferred product, process, or method against a predefined set of specifications as agreed upon with the sending unit and/or development unit."

A comparability exercise may be completed as an assessment of sending versus receiving process/method performance. Interim success criteria are developed to track progress toward these goals. Success is ultimately demonstrated by regulatory agency licensure in the desired region(s). In addition, business performance parameters are established to balance risk versus cost, including resources.

Evaluation of the success of a technology transfer should be based on a pre-established set of criteria, which are evaluated as the project progresses. These criteria may be used to track progress of the transfer into subsequent phases and hence manage risk.

Success criteria usually take into account the business situation and product requirements, for example:

  • Stage within the product lifecycle
  • Availability of product and process knowledge
  • Experience of the sending units and receiving units
  • Number of sites involved
  • Whether it is a transfer between internal sites or to an external site

From a business perspective, the success of a technology transfer is based on efficiently meeting the requirements of product quality, patient safety, and efficacy, and business requirements. Business requirements may include:

  • Cost, including capital cost, expense and Cost of Goods Manufactured (COGM) targets
  • Capacity/volume
  • Equipment and facility capabilities
  • Time frames
  • Risk management
  • Regulatory requirements or strategy, including meeting existing commitments
  • Supply chain strategy

Success criteria can take several forms and may be dependent on the technology being transferred and the phase of development. The criteria should be measurable and achievable. Success criteria may include:

  • Evaluation of the technology performance
  • Adherence to the project timeline
  • Adherence to the budget

Specific success criteria should be documented in the technology transfer plan. Main aspects may include:

  • Process performance — comparing in-process data (either traditional or PAT generated) with historical data
  • Product quality that meets pre-established criteria (data sets for comparability analyses)
  • Confirmation that the control strategy is executable
  • Confirmation that the product control strategy from the sending unit has been successfully delivered by the receiving unit, including meeting requirements of product CQAs and specifications
  • Process performance as expected based on historical data:
    • Large molecule examples: cell growth rates, titers, step yields, chromatogram profiles, impurity clearance
    • Small molecule examples: impurity levels (solvents, elemental impurities), quality attributes (dissolution), material attributes (particle size distribution), process parameters (compression force), process yield, and throughput
  • Analytical method transfer and equivalency
  • Successful routine operation over an agreed number of batches
  • Successful routine operation of facility and equipment (operability, labor, OEE)
  • Training of staff
  • HSE objectives achieved
  • Documentation fully and satisfactorily completed
  • Regulatory inspection outcomes and regulatory submission on time
  • Improvement of process robustness and efficiency (exact 1:1 transfers are rare)

Consideration should also be made to establish longer term criteria (e.g., during process validation Stage 3) following closure of the technology transfer report. Technology transfer studies may fail to predict variance inherent in longer term evaluations. Success criteria could include permitting natural material attribute variance or intentional material attribute variance.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 三維成功標準

ISPE 將技術轉移成功標準分為三個維度：

  • 技術層面（Technical）：製程性能是否符合規格？分析方法是否等效？
  • 法規層面（Regulatory）：是否取得目標市場的法規核准？法規提交是否準時？
  • 商業層面（Business）：成本（COGM）是否達標？時程是否符合？設備利用率（OEE）是否改善？

三個維度缺一不可。技術上成功但商業上虧損，或技術上成功但法規上被拒，都不算真正的成功。

比喻說明 Analogy

成功標準就像奧運競賽的評分規則——必須在比賽「開始前」公告，否則裁判（和選手）都不知道往哪個方向努力。技術轉移若等到最後才定義「什麼叫成功」，等同於比賽結束後才宣布評分標準，必然引發爭議。

重點提示 Key Notes

可量化且可達成：成功標準必須是 measurable（可量化）且 achievable（可達成）的。「製程穩定」不是成功標準；「三批連續生產的 API 回收率 ≥ 95%，RSD < 2%」才是。

「一比一完美複製」是神話：指南明確指出，exact 1:1 transfers are rare。接收單位幾乎必然需要調整某些參數以適應自身設備。這意味著成功標準應允許合理的製程優化空間，而非要求零偏差。

長期標準不容忽視：短期 TT 報告關閉後，Stage 3 製程驗證期間的批次間變異可能比 TT 階段大。建議在 TT 計畫中就預先規劃長期監控指標。

成功標準框架 Success Criteria Framework

技術成功標準（Technical）
├─ 製程性能 vs. 歷史數據
│   ├─ 大分子：cell growth rates, titers, yields
│   └─ 小分子：impurities, dissolution, particle size
├─ 分析方法等效性（method equivalency）
└─ 控制策略可執行性

法規成功標準（Regulatory）
├─ 法規提交準時
├─ 可比性數據（comparability data）充分
└─ 法規機構審查通過

商業成功標準（Business）
├─ COGM 目標達成
├─ 時程達成率
├─ OEE 改善
└─ 員工訓練完成

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 在與客戶簽訂技術轉移合約前，應要求客戶提供（或共同定義）書面的成功標準，並明確區分「合約成功標準」（觸發付款里程碑）和「技術監控標準」（持續追蹤製程狀態）。前者通常較寬鬆（例如完成 3 批驗證），後者應更嚴格（批次間 CPP 一致性）。若客戶堅持不書面化成功標準，這是一個重要的紅旗訊號。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 請嘗試為一個無菌充填製程的技術轉移，各寫出一條可量化的技術、法規和商業成功標準。
  2. OEE（Overall Equipment Efficiency）在技術轉移成功標準中代表什麼？如何計算？
Chapter 3 — Technology Transfer Project Phases (Phases 1–3)｜第三章：技術轉移專案階段（第1-3階段）

原文內容 Original Text

This chapter provides a description for each of the six phases of a technology transfer. It is intended to be generic and describes general practices that apply to all transfers regardless of the technology being transferred. To note, at the time of publication, it is increasingly common for phases to overlap and/or be executed in parallel. The same principles used to manage and control a traditionally phased technology transfer can be leveraged for transfer with overlapping phases. The key principle in either case is to identify critical dependencies and control phase execution accordingly.

Figure 3.2 shows the six phases of technology transfer: Phase 1 — Form Transfer Team and Develop Charter Phase 2 — Consolidate Knowledge for Transfer and Develop TT Proposal Phase 3 — Identify Risks, Conduct Risk Assessments, Develop TT Plan Phase 4 — Execute Technology Transfer (covered in other chapters) Phase 5 — Confirm Technology Transfer Phase 6 — Close Technology Transfer

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

六階段框架：ISPE 將技術轉移分為六個有序但可能重疊的階段。本節涵蓋前三個規劃階段（Phase 1-3）。重要認知：指南承認在現實中各階段可能重疊執行（parallel execution），這反映了業界對縮短上市時間的壓力。關鍵原則是識別關鍵依存關係，而非強求線性順序。

重點提示 Key Notes

對 CDMO 而言，Phase 1-3 決定了整個專案是否「有一個好的開始」。這三個規劃階段若執行草率，Phase 4（執行）必然問題叢生——通常表現為：批次失敗、偏差處理爆炸、客戶投訴、成本超支。規劃投入的時間永遠比修復失誤的時間便宜。

Phase 1 (3.1) — Form Transfer Team and Develop Charter｜建立轉移團隊與制定章程

原文內容 Original Text

The initiation phase of technology transfer should establish the team, strategy, and goals of a project. Sending and receiving units should establish an integrated team of the required SMEs from the functional areas involved in the transfer. This team should develop a technology transfer charter to capture the goals, milestones, and roles and responsibilities for the project.

3.1.1 Establishing a Team

A formal technology transfer team should be established. The team structure, roles, and responsibilities should be identified. Team structure should include leadership from both sending units and receiving units, along with SMEs from the relevant functional areas.

At the start of the technology transfer program, key stakeholders, technical leads, and project managers should be identified. An overall project manager is usually responsible for delivery of the technology transfer and should coordinate activities such as finance, quality/regulatory, and materials management.

Technical leads are usually responsible for ensuring that project managers have the technical information to enable delivery of the technology transfer. Depending upon the complexity of the project, a technical lead and project manager may be the same person. If the lead serves this dual role, it is important to ensure that project management responsibilities cannot be neglected when competing priorities arise.

The core team should include representation from both the sending and receiving, as appropriate. Examples of functions represented in the core team include:

  • Analytical sciences / Analytical/Quality Control (QC)
  • Engineering
  • HSE and sustainability
  • Late stage development
  • Manufacturing operations / Manufacturing technical
  • Material management / Planning
  • Process development
  • Project management
  • QA
  • R&D
  • Regulatory affairs
  • Supply chain

Project stakeholders (e.g., senior management, budget managers) provide oversight and guidance. Examples of stakeholder functions: Finance, Manufacturing, Process development, Program management (commercial), Quality, R&D, Regulatory affairs, Technical services.

Technology transfer team leads and project stakeholders should define the appropriate governance and controls, generally covering:

  • Scope of the project
  • Timelines and key milestones
  • Resources and budget
  • Success criteria
  • Reporting and escalation structure
  • Key decision gates/approval process
  • Change and risk management processes
  • Quality management

Communication between the members of the team can be more effective when team members:

  • From both units have a similar level of knowledge and experience of the techniques involved
  • Have good team working skills
  • Have the time to ensure that actions from risk/gap assessment are progressed
  • Define mutually accepted means of communication and collaboration (face-to-face kickoffs + regular teleconferences)
  • Acknowledge and manage cultural differences

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Project Manager vs. Technical Lead：這兩個角色在技術轉移中有不同職責。PM 管交付、時程、資源協調；Technical Lead 管技術正確性。指南提醒，若由同一人兼任，當技術問題緊急時，PM 職責容易被排擠——這是很常見的失敗模式。

Core Team vs. Stakeholders：核心團隊（Core Team）是日常執行者，利害關係人（Stakeholders）是監督和提供資源的高層。兩者都必須在 Phase 1 就識別，確保資源和決策支持。

比喻說明 Analogy

技術轉移團隊就像一場外科手術：主刀醫師（Technical Lead）專注技術執行；麻醉師、護士、協調員各司其職；手術室主任（Project Manager）確保整個流程順暢。如果主刀醫師還要兼任協調員，手術品質必然下降。

重點提示 Key Notes

QA 的角色：請注意，QA 被列在核心團隊（core team），而非只是利害關係人。這意味著 QA 應在 Phase 1 就深度參與，而非在 Phase 4 執行時才被動審查文件。早期 QA 參與可以預防大量後期的合規問題。

Regulatory Affairs 同在核心團隊：技術轉移的法規策略（哪些變更需要申請，哪些可以年度報告）必須從 Phase 1 就確定方向，不能等到快驗證完才詢問 RA 團隊。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 內部應建立「技術轉移 RACI 模板」，明確在每個階段，QA、RA、工程、分析等各部門各自的 Responsible / Accountable 角色。建議在每個新案的 Kick-off Meeting 上正式確認這份 RACI，並記錄在 meeting minutes 中。這份文件之後可作為爭議仲裁的基礎。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在您的組織中，技術轉移的 PM 和 Technical Lead 是同一人嗎？這樣的安排帶來哪些挑戰？
  2. 哪些功能部門最常在技術轉移的核心團隊中缺席，而事後造成問題？
3.1.2 Developing a Charter｜制定技術轉移章程

原文內容 Original Text

The technology transfer team may develop a technology transfer charter. The charter can include:

  • Assumptions and constraints
  • Sites impacted (sending and receiving) — scope including overview of the project and business drivers; items out of scope are equally important to document
  • Objectives and technical success criteria (see Chapter 2) — e.g., number of batches required, anticipated yield, successful registration and launch
  • Roles and responsibilities — clear understanding of expectations for each leadership role, deliverables for functional areas (documentation, testing, disposition, stability)
  • Technology transfer team — who is within the team from each unit, sub-team requirements, meeting frequency
  • Governance — definition of decision rights and escalation path
  • High level technology transfer plan:
    • Timescales and resource requirements from each functional group
    • Communication strategy
    • Risk assessment review (including HSE)
    • Technology transfer documentation expectations
    • Analytical transfer process and timelines
    • Commissioning and validation of additional technology or infrastructure
    • Manufacturing plan and sampling requirements
    • Data review plan, including deviation (non-conformance) reporting obligations between sending and receiving units
  • Regulatory strategy
  • Change control procedure
  • Technology transfer completions and formal transfer to clinical and/or commercial operations
"Note: Typically, deviations are reported back to the sending unit to facilitate support in review and for applicable development of corrective actions. However, if the sending unit is, for example, in production, utilizing methods transferred, under regulatory agency review, etc., then sending to receiving reporting will be equally important."

The technology transfer charter should be reviewed and approved by the appropriate stakeholders, executive sponsors, and senior management from both the sending and receiving units.

Note: The technology transfer charter and proposal may be either the same document or the charter may be versioned, depending on the complexity of the technology transfer project.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — Charter 的本質

Charter（章程）：是技術轉移啟動的正式協議文件，通常是高層次的「合作框架」，而非詳細的執行計畫。Charter 確立的是「Why（為何轉移）、Who（誰負責什麼）、What（轉移範疇）、When（關鍵里程碑）」，而非技術細節的「How」。

Charter vs. TT Proposal vs. TT Plan：
Charter = 高層次框架協議（1-5頁，供高層簽署）
TT Proposal = 詳細技術要求文件（覆蓋 Phase 2）
TT Plan = 逐項執行計畫（覆蓋 Phase 3）

比喻說明 Analogy

Charter 就像是建築工程的「合約書」，TT Proposal 是「設計圖」，TT Plan 是「施工日誌」。三者功能不同，不能互相替代。很多 CDMO 犯的錯誤是把所有東西塞進一份「TT Protocol」，結果既不夠高層也不夠細緻，合約談不清楚，技術也沒說明白。

重點提示 Key Notes

「Out of Scope」同樣重要：指南特別強調，不在轉移範疇內的事項同樣需要書面化在 Charter 中。這防止日後客戶（送出單位）要求「這個不也應該包含在轉移裡嗎？」——明確的 out-of-scope 是 CDMO 防範範疇蔓延（scope creep）的重要工具。

偏差雙向回報：注意指南要求，偏差（deviation）不只由接收單位向送出單位報告，若送出單位也在使用同一套方法或製程，則反向報告也同樣重要。CDMO 應在 Quality Agreement 和 Charter 中明確規定這個雙向溝通機制。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的 CDMO 目前使用的技術轉移啟動文件是 Charter、Protocol 還是其他名稱？它是否包含了上述所有要素？
  2. 若客戶在 TT 進行到一半時提出「這個功能也應該包含在轉移裡」，您如何利用 Charter 的 out-of-scope 條款處理？
Phase 2 (3.2) — Consolidate Knowledge & Develop Technology Transfer Proposal｜整合知識與制定技術轉移提案

原文內容 Original Text

3.2.1 Technology Transfer Proposal

A technology transfer proposal may be useful to define, facilitate review, and garner agreement of incomplete elements of the charter. In addition, prior to developing a detailed execution plan, a proposal can be used to develop detailed requirements and acceptance criteria for either key, or yet undefined, aspects of the plan.

The items listed below are recommended for inclusion in the technology transfer proposal:

  • HSE required assessments and known impacts
  • Overview of project and business drivers
  • List of team members and management/budget approvers (stakeholders)
  • Broad objectives and deliverables — projected clinical manufacture (successful number of runs), agreed process upgrades, successful registration
  • High level timeline and resources needed — divided into phases with "approval to proceed" at each phase end; realistic timeline (not assuming 100% success); significant capital requirements and estimated FTE; responsibility for funding
  • Issue resolution pathways and governance, including escalation
  • Validation strategy
  • Regulatory strategy — product/process comparability, stability, process validation; regulatory agency meetings and filing dates
  • Assumptions — raw material availability, successful analytics transfer, acceptable process changes, data system compatibility, facility fit, site utilities
  • Potential risks — FTE competition, unfavorable clinical/regulatory outcomes, gaps in process understanding, inability to mitigate facility fit, limitations in analytical support, comparability issues
  • Identification of information needed for the technology transfer package
  • Opportunities for receiving unit personnel to observe the process at the sending unit (tacit knowledge)
  • Requirements for disposition, storage, shipping, and forward processing

Note: Where a drug substance or drug product has received a marketing authorization, the regulatory strategy may be a key contributory factor in the strategic intent of the project.

Both the sending unit and the receiving unit should review and agree on the technology transfer proposal.

3.2.2 Technology Transfer Package

The technology transfer package should be organized efficiently to provide easy access to necessary information. It should also be comprehensive, so that a receiving unit can become self-sufficient in running a process or analytical procedure.

Basic requirements for the technology transfer package include:

  • HSE related requirements — prioritize HSE impact assessments early (long lead activities such as facility modification, regional licenses, training/monitoring programs)
  • Business requirements
  • Product specific requirements, particularly CQAs and control strategy and how these will be delivered at the receiving unit
"Note: It is not the role of technology transfer to identify quality attributes and process parameters and their relationships; this is the basis of the control strategy which is typically defined during process development. The control strategy is required to be available to the receiving unit to provide the scientific rationale which supports the manufacturing process and supporting analytical methods."
  • Process flow diagrams, unit operations, parameters and material attributes, design space (where used), process trends, detailed historical data (including sequence and justification of any process changes), risk assessments, identified CPPs and CQAs
  • Facilities capabilities assessment relative to the ability to implement and consistently execute requirements of the control strategy

The technology transfer team should review the completed technology transfer package and request SME input, as appropriate, to ensure that all relevant knowledge is captured. The team should also summarize the available knowledge and conduct a high level technical risk assessment.

The technology transfer team should ensure that the receiving unit understands the information available and can obtain clarifications. The knowledge transfer should take into account the level of expertise at both units.

For transfers to an external partner or CMO, the transferring organization should determine what kinds of intellectual property it would consider to be confidential and determine how to redact documents appropriately.

The technology transfer package information will be used by team members to work on a detailed process description and list of requirements for the receiving unit to execute the process. The team should then work through this list as part of a gap analysis, to identify, assign scores (if needed), and propose mitigation activities for gaps. The information gathered from the process description and gap analysis should be incorporated into a detailed technology transfer plan.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — TT Package 的「食譜」本質

Technology Transfer Package（技術轉移套件）：這是讓接收單位能夠獨立執行製程的完整知識集合。必要的核心內容包括：

  • 製程描述與歷史（含所有製程變更的理由）
  • CPP 設定值與可接受範圍
  • CQA 規格與管控策略
  • 分析方法及設備規格
  • 已知失效模式（known failure modes）
  • 設計空間（如有）
  • 設施能力評估

若任何一項缺失，接收單位就像拿到一份缺頁食譜——可能做出來，但必然存在隱患。

比喻說明 Analogy

TT Package 就像是特許加盟連鎖店（franchise）給加盟主的「完整操作手冊」。手冊必須詳細到讓新加盟主即使從未接受過親自訓練，也能做出與總部相同水準的產品。若手冊缺少某個秘密醬料的配方，那個加盟店的出品必然不達標。

重點提示 Key Notes

TT 不是用來「定義」CQA 的：指南明確提醒，技術轉移的目的是「傳遞」控制策略，而非「建立」它。CQA 和製程參數之間的關係應在製程開發階段就已確定。若 CDMO 承接的案子，送出單位連 CQA 都說不清楚，這是一個嚴重的紅旗——代表送出單位的製程理解本身就不充分。

IP 機密性管理：對外部 CMO（即 CDMO）的轉移，送出單位需要決定哪些資訊屬於機密 IP，並進行適當的文件脫敏（redact）。CDMO 應在合約中明確要求獲得「足夠執行製程的完整資訊」，同時尊重客戶的 IP 保護需求。必要時，以技術諮詢服務費取代文件交付。

TT Package 核心內容清單

必備（Must Have）
├─ 製程描述 + 製程歷史（含變更理由）
├─ CPP 設定值、範圍、設計空間
├─ CQA 規格 + 控制策略科學根據
├─ 分析方法 + 設備規格（HPLC 型號等）
├─ 已知失效模式（risk register）
└─ HSE 要求與特殊操作說明

應備（Should Have）
├─ 供應商資訊（原料、試劑）
├─ 製程流程圖（PFD）
├─ 設施能力評估報告
└─ 前次驗證/確認摘要

建議備（Nice to Have）
├─ 操作技巧說明（tacit knowledge 文件化）
└─ 歷史批次數據（APR/PQR 摘要）

實務應用 Practical Application

建議 CDMO 建立一份標準「TT Package 查核清單」，在每個新案的 Phase 2 開始時，由接收單位 QA + 技術主管共同審核送出單位提供的資料是否完整。清單中每一項都必須有明確的「已收到 / 待補充 / 不適用」狀態，並追蹤補充時限。這個清單後來可作為 Gap Analysis 的輸入。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若客戶（送出單位）告知「設計空間文件尚未建立，只有歷史批次數據」，您會如何調整 TT Package 的要求和後續風險評估？
  2. TT Proposal 中「假設事項（Assumptions）」的清單為何重要？若某個假設後來被證明不成立，應如何處理？
Phase 3 (3.3) — Identify Risks, Conduct Risk Assessments & Develop TT Plan｜識別風險、執行風險評估與制定轉移計畫

原文內容 Original Text

Following approval of a proposal for the technology transfer and exchange of the technology transfer package, the transfer team should perform risk assessments on identified gaps between the process or procedure requirements and the receiving unit capabilities and practices.

The technology transfer package can be used by both units to initiate risk assessments and begin developing the technology transfer plan for process or method implementation, along with the information, data, or work that will be required to ensure the technology can be successfully executed at the receiving unit. These assessments should compare the process or procedure history with the receiving unit capabilities and operations to identify gaps or misalignments that will require modifications.

In addition, the receiving unit should perform assessments of the following:

  • Process/method performance and validation packages
  • Raw materials/reagents for supply risk
  • Impact of incoming technology
  • Impact of changes needed as part of the implementation

This planning phase concludes once the sending and receiving units have completed the required assessments and have initiated plans to either remediate identified risks or receive risk acceptance from an appropriate governance.

Planning and execution of a technology transfer should include a comprehensive risk assessment process (i.e., risk identification, risk analysis, and risk evaluation as per ICH Q9), followed by risk control (i.e., risk reduction and risk acceptance) and development of a detailed action plan to mitigate risks.

"As part of a technology transfer, QRM is the documented procedure by which differences between sending unit and receiving unit can be identified and managed. Risk assessment is the process by which the criticalities of these differences are qualitatively or quantitatively estimated and prioritized. Once key gaps that require mitigation of risk are determined, a specific action plan for each gap should be defined and performed as part of the technology transfer execution."

The aim of QRM is to lower risks to acceptable levels. Where this is not possible or readily achievable, the risks are presented to the stakeholders for their approval to proceed "at risk" to the process qualification stage. Any differences between the sending unit and the receiving unit have the potential to increase risk to the receiving unit's ability to demonstrate product realization, cause delays, increase technology transfer costs, and have negative business impacts.

Sufficient time should be provided before technology transfer execution to identify and address differences. The sending unit and the receiving unit should perform these activities to help to improve knowledge transfer. These activities can promote teambuilding and improve future communication during later stages of a technology transfer.

It is usually preferable to address issues prior to the process qualification exercise, as opposed to during. For instance, if a process change is required due to conditions/constraints at the receiving unit, risk could be better defined and potentially mitigated by conducting studies in the small scale process model to examine the effects of the change.

It is advised that risk identification, risk analysis, and mitigation be conducted as early as possible since some risk mitigation activities may have long lead times and thus could significantly delay technology transfer. Although site selection is not discussed in this Guide, facility fit and site expertise are important factors to consider as they can have significant impact on the timeline and costs.

This risk assessment should be used to define the overall transfer approach.

3.3.1 Identifying Risks

As noted in Section 1.2, effective knowledge management (including tacit knowledge) is critical for effective risk management. Teams are advised to critically review information and knowledge utilized in risk identification, e.g., gaps in development reports.

Identification of risks is typically performed by appropriate SMEs and ad hoc members from the sending unit and the receiving unit (i.e., process/technical experts, manufacturing, quality, facility and process engineers, automation, materials/procurement, HSE, analytical, Chemistry, Manufacturing, and Controls (CMC) regulatory, etc.).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — Gap Analysis 的邏輯

Gap Analysis（差距分析）：系統性比較送出單位製程要求（what is needed）與接收單位現有能力（what is available）之間的差距。差距可能來自：

  • 設備差距：接收單位使用不同廠牌/型號的設備，其操作原理可能不同
  • 原料差距：同一原料可能來自不同供應商，規格略有差異
  • 分析平台差距：HPLC 系統、管柱型號、軟體版本不同
  • 法規歷史差距：接收單位可能沒有送出單位的法規核准歷史
  • 人員能力差距：接收單位人員對特定技術的熟悉程度

比喻說明 Analogy

Phase 3 的 Gap Analysis 就像搬家前的「家具清點」：你在新家有什麼？你需要把什麼從舊家搬過去？什麼需要新買？哪些舊東西在新家放不下？這個清點工作必須在搬家前（Phase 3）完成，而非搬進去後才發現床根本進不了門（Phase 4 批次失敗）。

風險類別框架 Risk Category Framework

技術風險（Technical Risk）
├─ 製程穩健性（process robustness）
├─ 設備等效性（equipment equivalency）
├─ 原料相容性（raw material compatibility）
└─ 分析方法轉移等效性

組織風險（Organizational Risk）
├─ 知識流失（knowledge loss / staff turnover）
├─ 人員能力缺口
└─ 文化差異造成的溝通障礙

法規風險（Regulatory Risk）
├─ 變更申請要求（variation filing）
├─ 可比性數據需求
└─ 不同市場的法規差異

時程風險（Timeline Risk）
├─ 長前置期活動（long lead items）
├─ 關鍵路徑延誤
└─ 資源競爭（FTE competition）

重點提示 Key Notes

「先做小規模研究」的黃金原則：若接收單位因設備或條件限制需要製程變更，指南建議在小規模模型中先研究變更的影響，而非直接在 GMP 批次中實驗。這在 CDMO 的無菌充填轉移中特別重要——灌裝參數調整應先在工程批（engineering run）中驗證。
