「At Risk」決策：若某些風險無法在執行前完全緩解，必須由適當的治理層級（governance）正式批准「帶風險進行」（proceed at risk）。這個決策必須書面記錄，不能是口頭協議。CDMO 在接受此類「at risk」決策時，應確保客戶（送出單位高層）也簽署確認，明確風險由誰承擔。

長前置期活動要提早識別：某些風險緩解行動本身就需要很長時間（如設備採購、法規申請、原料供應商轉換）。若到 Phase 3 才發現這些需求，可能已無法在既定時程內完成。Phase 2 結束時就應初步識別這些長前置期項目。

實務應用 Practical Application — CDMO 接收單位視角

CDMO 在執行 Phase 3 時，建議從四個維度系統性評估風險：

  • 技術維度：比對設備規格表、確認製程參數範圍是否在接收設備的操作能力內
  • 分析維度：確認每個分析方法所需的設備型號、試劑、管柱是否與接收單位一致
  • 法規維度：確認在目標市場，此次設備/地點變更是否觸發變更申請，預估審批時間
  • 人員維度：評估操作團隊對此技術的熟悉程度，制定培訓計畫

每個識別的差距應在 Risk Register 中記錄：差距描述、嚴重性評分（S）、發生機率（O）、可偵測性（D）、計算 RPN，以及提議的緩解行動和負責人/完成時限。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在無菌充填製程的技術轉移中，哪類風險（技術、組織、法規、時程）通常是最難提前識別的？
  2. 若送出單位同意「帶風險進行」，CDMO 應如何在合約中保護自己，確保風險責任清晰？
  3. 長前置期活動（long lead items）的典型例子有哪些？如何在 Phase 2 就提早識別？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 成功標準三維度：技術（製程性能、方法等效）+ 法規（可比性數據、提交準時）+ 商業（COGM、時程、OEE）— 必須在轉移開始前書面定義，不能事後才評定。
  • 文件層次：Charter（高層協議，含 out-of-scope 條款）→ TT Proposal（詳細要求）→ TT Plan（逐項執行計畫）。三者功能不同，混用會導致範疇蔓延。
  • TT Package 是轉移成敗的關鍵：必須涵蓋製程歷史、CPP/CQA、控制策略、分析方法、已知失效模式、設施評估。任何缺失都是潛在的批次失敗種子。
  • Gap Analysis 系統化：從設備、原料供應商、分析平台、法規歷史四個維度比對差距，每個差距在 Risk Register 中記錄嚴重性、機率、可偵測性和緩解行動。
  • 長前置期項目提早識別：Phase 3 中任何緩解行動若需要超過 4 週的準備時間，應立即列為高優先級並啟動，否則將成為整個時程的瓶頸。
  • QA 與 RA 從 Phase 1 就深度參與：而非等到執行後才審查，是縮短整體 TT 週期、避免後期補救的關鍵實踐。
2

Chapter 2: TT Project Phases 4–6: Operational Readiness to Finalization (Ch 3b)

技術轉移第4-6階段：操作準備至完成審查 | p41-p52

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Technology Transfer (3rd Edition) | p41–p52

本章學習目標

  • 理解「操作準備度」（Operational Readiness）的五大支柱，以及為何它是技術轉移延誤最常發生的根源
  • 區分工程試驗（Engineering Runs）與製程性能確認（PPQ）批次的本質差異及法規意涵
  • 掌握分析方法可比性（Analytical Comparability）的統計驗證邏輯，了解 ICH Q2(R1) 的應用場景
  • 明確定義「轉移完成」的法律與操作標準，以及 Phase 6 結束後送出方（Sending Unit）的持續義務
  • 從 CDMO 角度，了解如何在合約中明確界定技術支援範圍與智慧財產邊界
3.4 Operational Readiness — 操作準備度

原文內容 Original Text ISPE TT 3rd Ed.

3.4 Operational Readiness

The goal of the operational readiness phase is to achieve a state of readiness required to move into the qualification phase, as described in Section 3.5. Both the process and methods are required to be in a state of control prior to entering qualification phase. A critical review of the operational readiness should be performed and formally documented.

Analytical methods are required to be qualified prior to full scale process qualification in order to be able to measure process performance. In some cases, method qualification may be concurrent with process qualification; in this case, the risk to the overall qualification risk must be documented and accepted by management.

Closure of actions defined by gap analysis and corresponding risk assessments drive the requirements to complete this phase.

Operational readiness activities required may include:

  • Additional process or method development
  • Equipment installation, modification, or re-validation
  • General commissioning, qualification and validations as needed (refer to ISPE Baseline® Guide: Commissioning and Qualification)
  • Engineering runs
  • Procurement
  • Training runs or training of staff

Having identified gaps and risks, then subsequently prioritizing activities, technology transfer operational readiness may include the following:

  • Facility modifications identified in risk identification/gap analysis, including appropriate equipment validations
  • Testing of full scale manufacturing equipment to ensure proper function, e.g., mixing studies, buffer or water runs, cleaning studies, etc.

In the case of cleaning, it is recommended that a comprehensive review of the requirements (e.g., soil types, required cleanability limits, and methods of detection) are compiled into a planning document. It is highly likely that changes in equipment type, scale-up, and process optimization implemented during the transfer will require new cleaning and monitoring methods, sample types, and corresponding analytical method qualifications.

As noted in Sections 2.2 and 3.3.1, effective knowledge management is crucial throughout all the previous phases. Operation readiness requires generation of documentation at the receiving unit required to implement and control changes necessary for implementation of the transferred process and/or methods. Diligence in document review and reconciliation in this phase is of paramount importance prior to proceeding to the qualification phase.

Examples of required documentation are as follows:

  • Flow chart of process steps
    • Quantities of all materials and stoichiometry of the starting materials, intermediates, and reagents
    • Specific processing conditions (e.g., times, temperatures, and pressures)
    • Sequence of activities (e.g., order of addition of reagents)
    • Expected theoretical yield and output weight/volume of product
    • CPPs, i.e., factors impacting product quality
    • Permitted tolerance ranges for key parameters (e.g., yield impacting parameters)
    • Detail of other materials and by-products generated and their fate
    • Mass balance information
  • Development and approval of receiving unit manufacturing instruction documents (batch records, SOPs, automation recipes, etc.)
    • A clearly defined structure for review and approval of the manufacturing documents should be agreed upon by the sending unit and receiving unit, including expectations for duration and number of reviews. A well-organized system for tracking and managing edits throughout the process should be used by the teams.
  • Implementation of small scale laboratory models at receiving unit
    • As part of the transfer, small scale models of some or all the unit operations may be transferred to the receiving unit. These can be used for process training before large scale runs begin, for additional process development work identified in the risk identification/gap analysis, and can also be used for efficient troubleshooting during the initial large scale runs.
    • A suggested practice is to use the small scale model in a "satellite" mode alongside the initial large scale runs with the same buffers or media. This can help to troubleshoot problems that may be observed at scale by providing a control for some of the parameters.
    • An overall assessment comparing the small scale runs to the production runs should be documented or referenced in a campaign summary report.
  • Process training
    • Training should be conducted by SMEs prior to the start of the GMP campaign. It may be helpful to have some elements of this training led by personnel from the sending unit where they may have more extensive process experience. It also may be useful to have personnel from the sending unit as support staff during operation of first full scale batch.
  • Models
    • Various models can be used by companies to develop pharmaceutical products. The rigor and documentation associated with the technical transfer of such models should be commensurate with the complexity and risk associated with their implementation and intended use.
    • Where models are established only for the purpose of understanding a process and its unit operations, it is usually sufficient to transfer the model as part of the knowledge base for the product, as these models are not part of ongoing control decisions during production. Where models are established as elements of a control strategy for ongoing production, consideration should be given to scale, sampling, and instrument dependencies as applicable.
    • In addition, procedures to calibrate, verify, maintain, if applicable validate, and update models should be established, as appropriate to the nature of the model being used.
  • Creation of real time processing models and data trending template
  • Identification of in-process controls for monitoring
  • Cleaning requirements per process step, including required analysis and forward processing criteria
  • Generation of sample plan

In a GMP environment, some of these activities may require additional risk assessments and change controls as a part of the activity.

Additionally, the operational readiness phase of the technology transfer project will include the generation of the documentation and/or electronic systems that will be used to execute the technology at the receiving unit. This activity should be supported through the information and deliverables that were included as a part of the technology transfer package generated in the pre-transfer planning phase.

The operational readiness phase of the technology transfer is complete when the process and analytical procedures are qualified. The sending and receiving units should be confident in the receiving unit's ability to successfully execute analytical procedures or manufacturing processes.

Following successful completion of the technology transfer operational readiness phase, the project will move into the process/procedure qualification phase of the project.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：操作準備度的五大支柱

ISPE 將 Operational Readiness（操作準備度）定義為「進入確認階段前必須達到的就緒狀態」。實務上，這可以分解為五個缺一不可的支柱：

  • 設備（Equipment）：安裝、確認（IQ/OQ/PQ）全部完成，清潔驗證已有計畫
  • 人員（Personnel）：製程 SME 完成培訓，GMP 記錄能力通過評估
  • 物料（Materials）：原料、耗材、標準品均已取得並合格，供應鏈就緒
  • 程序（Procedures）：批次記錄、SOP、自動化配方全部發布且經雙方審核
  • 法規（Regulatory）：必要的申請變更已提交，監管時間軸已確認

五個支柱全部亮綠燈才能啟動第一批次——這是最多延誤發生的地方。

比喻說明 Analogy

操作準備度就像醫院開刀房的「清單確認」流程：在開刀前，必須確認麻醉機（設備）可用、外科團隊（人員）到位、血袋（物料）準備好、手術程序（SOP）已核准、術前家屬同意書（法規文件）已簽妥。任何一項缺失，手術就不能開始——無論外科醫師多有經驗。技術轉移的第一批 GMP 批次，正是這台「手術」。

重點提示：為什麼大多數 TT 延誤發生在 Phase 4？

工程試驗（Engineering Runs）暴露真正的差距，而在 Phase 3 的風險識別中往往低估以下問題：

  • 清潔驗證方法在新設備幾何形狀下失效，需要重新開發分析方法
  • 原料資格（Vendor qualification）因供應商審核週期長而拖延
  • 批次記錄（BPR）的雙方審核輪次比預期多出 2-3 輪
  • 自動化配方在新平台移植後出現參數偏移，需要額外確認

給 CDMO 的警示：合約時程通常低估 Phase 4 的 buffer，這是最常見的商業糾紛來源。

實務應用：小規模衛星模型的 CDMO 戰略價值

ISPE 建議將小規模實驗室模型以「衛星模式」（satellite mode）與大規模生產同步運行。對 CDMO 而言，這個策略帶來三個競爭優勢：

  • 快速除錯：大規模批次出現異常時，可立即用小規模模型重現並隔離變數，不必等待下一批次
  • 知識留存：即使客戶撤出，CDMO 保有可執行的小規模模型，是未來再轉移的技術資產
  • 法規支援：衛星實驗室數據可作為 scale-down model 的確認依據，支持 FDA/EMA 的申請文件

重點提示：分析方法確認的時序風險

ISPE 明確指出：分析方法確認（Method Qualification）必須先於製程確認（Process Qualification）完成。若允許並行（concurrent），管理層必須正式接受並記錄此風險。

為何這是風險？若製程批次在方法尚未確認時啟動，萬一方法失效，批次結果將無法判讀——GMP 批次白跑，時間與成本雙輸。這正是清潔驗證分析方法轉移常被低估的陷阱。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若某 CDMO 在 Phase 4 發現設備清潔方法不適用於新型設備，最佳的風險處理路徑為何？是開始小規模清潔效果研究，還是直接要求客戶提供替代方法？
  2. 「衛星模式小規模模型」的數據需要多少才足以支持 Scale-down Model qualification？ICH Q5E 對生物製劑的可比性研究有何要求？
  3. 批次記錄的雙方審核輪次在合約中通常如何界定？超出輪次時，費用與時間責任應如何分配？
3.5 Process (Procedure) Qualification — 製程（程序）確認

原文內容 Original Text ISPE TT 3rd Ed.

3.5 Process (Procedure) Qualification

As noted in Section 3.3, a documented review of all readiness criteria and transfer requirements in the plan should be completed in a gated review with management oversight prior to proceeding to the process (procedure) qualification phase.

This phase may be executed through a demonstration of the technology at the receiving unit and a comparison of the process and product and data generated to ensure it aligns with expectations. This activity may be performed as a part of a formal qualification or validation exercise, in which case the data generated may be useful for supporting the regulatory approval processes.

The risk assessment from the technology transfer planning phases should be signed off and documented in accordance with the QMSs for both the sending and receiving units prior to proceeding to process (procedure) qualification. For further information, see ICH Q9 and the ISPE Guide Series: Product Quality Lifecycle Implementation (PQLI®). As previously noted in Section 3.3, risk assessments are most effective when utilized in phase gate reviews.

This phase should involve completion of the assessment of the data and product produced as a part of the transfer execution and identification of required mitigation plans to remediate any issues observed during qualification. The sending unit and receiving unit should define a plan for routine support of the technology at the receiving unit.

Execution of a qualification protocol should not begin until the protocol has been reviewed and approved by all appropriate departments, including the appropriate quality units. Any departures from the protocol should be made according to established quality procedures.

A report documenting and assessing adherence to the written qualification protocol should be prepared in a timely manner after the completion of the protocol. This report should:

  • Discuss and cross-reference all aspects of the protocol.
  • Summarize data collected and analyze the data, as specified by the protocol.
  • Evaluate any unexpected observations and additional data not specified in the protocol.
  • Summarize and discuss all non-conformances, such as deviations, aberrant test results, or other information that has bearing on the validity of the analytical procedure/process.
  • Describe in sufficient detail any corrective actions or changes that should be made to existing procedures and controls.
  • State a clear conclusion as to whether the data indicates the analytical procedure met the conditions established in the protocol and whether the analytical procedure is considered to be in a state of control. If not, the report should state what should be accomplished before such a conclusion can be reached.
  • Include all appropriate department and quality units review and approvals.
  • Provide the basis for continued process monitoring and control strategies.

It is recommended that a statistician or person with adequate training in statistical techniques help develop the data collection plan and any statistical methods and procedures used in measuring and evaluating the process or analytical method. If the process or analytical method qualification does not meet the acceptance criteria, the cause of the failure should be investigated and addressed before repeating the exercise.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：Engineering Runs vs. PPQ 批次

這是 Phase 5 最重要的概念區別：

特性 Engineering Runs PPQ 批次
GMP 狀態 非正式，可失敗 正式 GMP，不得隨意廢棄
法規用途 學習與調整 作為法規申請的核心證據
數量 視需要而定 通常最少 3 批（FDA 建議）
偏差處理 記錄即可 每個偏差均需完整調查
放行 不放行市場 合格時可放行市場

PPQ（Process Performance Qualification）（製程性能確認）是 FDA Process Validation Guidance 的第二階段，也是法規核准的關鍵依據。

比喻說明 Analogy

Engineering Runs 就像廚師在正式開幕前的「試菜日」——可以試錯、調整配方，不對顧客收費。PPQ 批次則像是餐廳的「開幕首日」——每道菜都要完美，主廚（QA）必須簽名，失敗紀錄會留在衛生稽查檔案中，而且這批菜（產品）是要出售給病患的。兩者的失敗代價截然不同。

分析方法可比性的統計框架

分析可比性 (Analytical Comparability) 核心問題：
接收單位的分析方法，能否產生與送出單位
「統計上等效」的結果？

驗證層次（依 ICH Q2(R1) 邏輯）：
1. 精確度比較 (Precision Comparison)
   RSD(接收) vs RSD(送出) — F-test or equivalence test

2. 準確度比較 (Accuracy/Bias Comparison)
   Mean bias = |μ接收 - μ送出| / μ送出 × 100%
   通常接受標準: bias < 2% (small molecule)
                       bias < 5% (bioassay)

3. 平台比較 (Platform Comparison)
   n 樣品在雙方實驗室同步分析 → paired t-test 或
   Bland-Altman plot — 視覺化系統偏差

4. 不確定度評估 (Measurement Uncertainty)
   EU Annex 15 / USP <1033> 要求量化不確定度

統計支援不可或缺：ISPE 明確建議由具備統計背景的人員設計數據收集計畫。

重點提示：Concurrent Validation 的法規態度

在某些情境（如罕見疾病、緊急需求），FDA 允許「同步驗證」（Concurrent Validation）——即在確認批次完成全部分析前即放行批次。但這要求：

  • 在申請檔案（BLA/NDA/ANDA）中明確說明理由
  • 有強健的即時放行測試（RTRT）控制策略
  • 後續確認結果必須追溯補回並形成報告

ISPE 在此強調：無論採用哪種策略，風險評估必須由管理層正式書面接受。CDMO 若接受此要求，必須在合約中明確保留撤回批次的權利。

實務應用：PPQ 報告的「六大必備」

ISPE 列出 PPQ 報告必須涵蓋的六個要素，對 CDMO 而言，這同時也是交付客戶的核心文件框架：

  • 全面對應協議（cross-reference all aspects of protocol）
  • 數據摘要與統計分析（summarize and analyze data）
  • 未預期觀察的評估（unexpected observations）
  • 不符合項完整清單（non-conformances, deviations）
  • 糾正行動說明（corrective actions）
  • 明確結論聲明（clear conclusion）

這六項缺一不可；FDA 483 觀察中，「PPQ 報告結論不明確」是常見警告項目。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 PPQ 第一批次出現一個 Critical Deviation（例如溫度超出規格），是否可以繼續執行第二批次，還是必須先完成 CAPA？ISPE 與 FDA 的立場各為何？
  2. 在生物製劑的技術轉移中，PPQ 批次通常需要幾批才足夠？「足夠」的判斷標準是什麼？
  3. 若接收單位的分析數據顯示系統偏差（systematic bias），但仍在規格內，這算轉移成功嗎？如何說服監管機構？
3.6 Finalize Transfer and Perform Review — 完成轉移與執行審查

原文內容 Original Text ISPE TT 3rd Ed.

3.6 Finalize Transfer and Perform Review

The final actions of the project should be focused on performing a review (sometimes called an after action review) to collect specific knowledge from the technology transfer. This should consider how each stage in the transfer went, how effective the communication and team work were, and whether any issues experienced during the qualification exercises were related to the effectiveness of the knowledge transfer.

The review may identify the need for a remediation plan and any ongoing support required from the sending unit. Where appropriate, key knowledge from the review should be shared with the teams involved in the technology transfer.

The complete evaluation of the success of the technology transfer through analysis of data or product (e.g., unexpected variability) generated as a part of the transfer execution will involve the sending and receiving units evaluating the performance of the technology, as well as the laboratory or manufacturing facility, and determining if any corrective action is required prior to declaring the transfer successful.

3.6.1 Planning for Transition of Support and Disengagement of Sending Unit

This can potentially include accountabilities and responsibilities for process or method improvements identified as a part of the transfer or through lifecycle management. There should be a clear transfer of responsibility to the receiving unit.

Agreement should be defined regarding the intended level of continuing support and involvement from the sending unit members of the technology transfer team.

Examples of aspects that should be considered for ongoing operations include:

  • The receiving unit will operate the specified process.
  • A change control procedure should be in place at the receiving unit.
  • Process deviations should be noted and evaluated for communication with the sending unit.
  • Process changes (continuous process improvement/lifecycle management) may be needed and initiated by either the sending or receiving unit. The initiated change must have prior agreement and be performed through a change control procedure. In some cases, process changes may require re-validation of the process. Global change control (e.g., when multiple sites are making the same product) is outside the scope of this document.
  • Process monitoring should be performed by the receiving unit. Any anomalous process trends should be evaluated for communication with the sending unit. If the product is manufactured at multiple sites, regular manufacturing review meetings should be conducted to troubleshoot processing problems between sites.

3.6.2 Support of Regulatory Activities

Post-transfer activities can include support of regulatory inspections or questions as a result of submissions associated with the transfer. Members from either the sending or receiving unit may be needed to provide assistance with regulatory activities by authoring documentation for filings or participating in site inspections.

3.6.3 Lessons Learned

An ongoing review during the transfer and/or a review at the conclusion of transfer phases that captures best practice and shared lessons learned should be performed. This should be documented and accessible to other teams from a continuous improvement perspective.

Where lessons learned are not captured during the execution of the transfer, a lessons learned meeting should be held as soon as possible after the completion of the process qualification. The meeting should provide an opportunity to review the technology transfer project and overall GMP performance. At a minimum, the meeting should involve members of the technology transfer team and focus on the successes and challenges faced throughout the project. It may be valuable to break out into specific areas that need to be addressed, for example:

  • Process
  • Documents
  • Analytics
  • Quality
  • Project management

The output from the meeting should be documented and shared with the technology transfer team.

The sending and receiving units should formally document lessons learned and determine future actions that would improve the success and efficiency of transfer projects or product commercialization.

Teams should strive to distinguish knowledge that is known (e.g., CQAs, CPPs, formal reports, Annual Product Review summaries, SOPs, etc.) from that which can be described as tacit (i.e., the knowledge that may be crucial for a successful transfer but is not actually written down.) Such tacit knowledge might include:

  • Historical knowledge
  • Informal knowledge
  • The way an operator or a laboratory analyst performs certain steps
  • Details of the order of operations, e.g. powder addition rates in the preparation of intermediates
  • The unusual operation of items of equipment
  • The actual way an operation is carried out (rather than just what the SOP says)
  • Ranges within which operations proven to be effective
  • Interventions
  • Other (non-critical) quality attributes or process parameters that might have an impact on, for example, ease of operation rather than directly impact product quality
  • Converting data into knowledge (e.g., data points can be plotted on a control chart and the knowledge is gained by assessing trends, limits, robustness, etc.)
  • Use of work arounds (which, in practice, should be built into formal procedures)
  • Taking learning from new events that arise (e.g., ensuring CAPAs do deliver the prevention as well as the correction)

It should be noted that ICH Q10 recommends knowledge to be managed over the whole product lifecycle.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：「轉移完成」的法律與操作定義

Phase 6 要回答一個核心問題：誰有權宣告轉移成功，以及依據什麼標準？

ISPE 建議轉移完成標準應包含：

  • 技術層面：PPQ 批次全部符合預設接受標準，無未關閉的 Critical OOS
  • 文件層面：技術轉移包（TTP）完整移交，知識轉移文件化
  • 組織層面：接收單位正式接管責任，變更控制已移交
  • 法規層面：相關申請（NDA/BLA Supplement 或 Site Change）已提交或獲批

關鍵教訓：若憲章（Charter）中未明確定義「誰」宣告完成，當雙方意見不一致時，商業糾紛不可避免。

比喻說明 Analogy

Phase 6 就像房屋交屋流程：不是工程完工就算完成，而是要有完整的「驗屋報告」（After Action Review）、明確的「交屋清單」（缺陷清單與責任分配）、以及「過戶登記」（法律責任轉移）。少了任何一個環節，房子雖然蓋好了，法律上還沒「交到你手上」。技術轉移亦然——PPQ 通過，不等於法律上「轉移完成」。

重點提示：送出方解除義務的三個條件

ISPE 3.6.1 強調：送出方（Sending Unit）的脫離（Disengagement）需要有明確合約支撐，且必須滿足三個前提：

  • 技術責任轉移：接收方已有獨立的製程改善與偏差處理能力
  • 變更控制機制就位：接收方已建立 Change Control 程序，且雙方對未來製程改變的溝通義務有書面共識
  • 監測責任移交：製程監測（Process Monitoring）數據的異常通報義務已明確定義

CDMO 警示：「技術轉移完成後，客戶還有問題找上門」是常見爭議。合約中必須明定 Phase 6 後的技術支援費率與義務上限。

核心概念：顯性知識 vs. 隱性知識

ISPE 在 3.6.3 提出了最重要的知識管理挑戰——隱性知識（Tacit Knowledge）的轉移。

顯性知識（Explicit Knowledge）可以寫在文件裡：CQA 清單、CPP 範圍、SOP、驗證報告。

隱性知識（Tacit Knowledge）在 SOP 裡找不到，但對成功至關重要，例如：

  • 「這台設備的攪拌軸有輕微振動，所以轉速要設在 85% 而非 100%」
  • 「粉末加料速率要在最後 5 分鐘降低，否則溶解度不一致」
  • 「分析師在取樣時習慣等 30 秒穩定期，但 SOP 只寫立即取樣」

這些知識若未轉移，PPQ 可能通過，但後續生產批次的良率會系統性低於送出方水準。

Lessons Learned 會議的結構化框架

Lessons Learned 五維分析框架：

維度          | 關鍵問題
-------------|----------------------------------
製程(Process)| 哪些製程步驟轉移最困難？為何？
文件(Docs)   | 哪些文件品質不足？審核效率如何？
分析(Analytics)| 方法轉移是否準時？哪些指標偏移？
品質(Quality)| OOS / Deviation 發生根本原因？
專案管理(PM) | 時程偏差發生在哪個 Phase？為何？

區別觀察（Observation）vs. 教訓（Lesson Learned）：
- 觀察 = 發現問題但無行動 → 下次仍會重演
- 教訓 = 發現問題 + 優先排序 + 行動計畫 + 追蹤監控

實務應用：CDMO 的 Phase 6 合約策略

技術轉移完成後，CDMO 通常面臨客戶要求的兩大「後轉移義務」：

  • 法規稽查支援（3.6.2）：客戶申請獲批前的 FDA/EMA 回應。CDMO 必須在合約中明定支援範圍（幾小時內回應？誰負責撰寫回應文件？費用如何計算？）
  • 配方/製程更新：若原廠在轉移後更新製程，CDMO 是否有義務重新確認？費用歸誰？

建議在 TT Charter 中明確加入：「Phase 6 完成後，超出範疇的技術支援應按 [費率表] 另行計費，客戶有義務提供最新製程更新資訊，延遲提供者不得主張 CDMO 違約。」

重點提示：ICH Q10 的知識管理要求

ISPE 引用 ICH Q10 第 1.6.1 節的重要聲明：知識管理必須涵蓋從開發到商業生命週期直至停產的全程。技術轉移活動本身就是知識管理的一環。這表示：

  • 轉移過程中產生的數據和知識屬於產品知識，必須系統性保存
  • ICH Q10 合規性要求 CDMO 建立知識管理系統（不只是文件管理系統）
  • Annual Product Review（APR）必須能追溯至 TT 期間建立的基準數據

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 Lessons Learned 會議發現某個製程風險在 Phase 3 就被識別，但因為優先順序低而未採取行動，最終在 PPQ 造成偏差——這屬於「教訓」還是「觀察」？下一步行動應為何？
  2. 送出方 SME 在 Phase 6 完成後三個月離職，帶走了大量隱性知識。接收單位此時應如何應對？這是誰的責任？合約中應如何預防？
  3. 客戶在技術轉移完成後提出要求：因為原廠更新了一個關鍵原料的規格，需要 CDMO 重新驗證。這屬於 TT 合約範圍內還是範圍外？你的論點為何？
3.6.3.1 Transfer of Ownership and Closure — 所有權移交與結案

原文內容 Original Text ISPE TT 3rd Ed.

3.6.3.1 Transfer of Ownership and Closure

Upon completion of technology transfer, a final assessment of the remaining risks should be conducted and documented as part of technology transfer close-out. A review should be conducted by the technical transfer team in order to document and agree that all critical issues have been resolved, knowledge transfer is documented, and any outstanding items have been assigned for owners to resolve.

Successful technology transfer should ensure that all high risks have been addressed and justification has been documented as to why some residual risks are acceptable and agreed by the receiving unit. At the time, any additional support that is required should be agreed to by the receiving unit.

An important step to improve future technology transfers is for the receiving unit to provide feedback to the sending unit. Depending on the cycle times of technology transfer, production schedules, and regulatory agency filings, this feedback may occur during the transfer, throughout PPQ and during regulatory agency driven events such as filings and inspections.

ICH Q10, Section 1.6.1: "Product and process knowledge should be managed from development through the commercial life of the product up to and including product discontinuation. For example, development activities using scientific approaches provide knowledge for product and process understanding. Knowledge management is a systematic approach to acquiring, analysing, storing and disseminating information related to products, manufacturing processes and components. Sources of knowledge include, but are not limited to prior knowledge (public domain or internally documented); pharmaceutical development studies; technology transfer activities; process validation studies over the product lifecycle; manufacturing experience; innovation; continual improvement; and change management activities."

The following ISPE concept papers provide useful supporting information and refer to technology transfer and knowledge management:

  • ISPE Concept Paper: Implementing Knowledge Management in Bioprocess
  • ISPE Concept Paper: The Role of Process Capability in Monitoring Product Quality

The ISPE Cultural Excellence Report also has some indicators regarding the importance of knowledge.

It is important for the team to distinguish between observations and true lessons learned. The key distinction is the effectiveness and sustainability of the actions taken related to the observation. The following points are offered as a tool for teams to distinguish lessons learned from observations:

  • Lessons learned could include observation, prioritization, and an action and monitoring plan.
  • Observations without actions can result in reoccurrence of the respective event. Depending on the impact of reoccurrence, CAPAs may be developed and tracked in a company's QMS.
  • Collect "work arounds" can be short term solutions but are often an unsustainable means to maintain performance.

Communication of the observations to the appropriate stakeholders, particularly to the receiving unit, should be confirmed prior to conclusion of the technology transfer project. In addition, it is recommended that the receiving unit manage a decision process for which observations warrant action plans and tracking.

Lessons learned documentation may be in addition to corrective actions captured and tracked through a QMS.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：結案的三道門檻

ISPE 3.6.3.1 定義了技術轉移正式結案（Close-out）的三個必要條件：

  1. 所有 Critical Issue 已解決：轉移團隊書面確認，無懸而未決的高風險項目
  2. 殘餘風險有書面理由：不是「沒有風險」，而是「殘餘風險已被接收方知情同意接受」
  3. 未完成項目已有責任人：Outstanding items 不能無主，必須指定擁有者與完成期限

缺少任何一項，技術轉移在法律與 GMP 意義上均不算完成。

比喻說明 Analogy

結案就像建築工程的「竣工驗收」：不是所有問題都解決了才驗收，而是所有重大缺陷必須修正，次要缺陷允許在約定期限內補正，並由承包方書面列清單、載明責任。若沒有正式驗收程序，日後業主與承包方的糾紛就只能靠記憶與口頭說法——這在 GMP 世界中是完全不可接受的。

重點提示：殘餘風險的「知情接受」原則

ISPE 的用字很精確：「justification has been documented as to why some residual risks are acceptable and agreed by the receiving unit」。這有兩層含義：

  • 可接受性有理由（Justified）：不能只寫「風險低」，要說明為什麼低、有何數據支持
  • 接收方知情同意（Agreed）：接收方 QA 和管理層必須書面簽名確認接受，否則未來出事時責任歸屬不清

這正是 ICH Q9 風險管理中「風險溝通（Risk Communication）」的核心要求。

技術轉移結案清單（Close-out Checklist）

Phase 6 正式結案必備文件清單：

[ ] PPQ 報告 — 已核准，結論明確
[ ] 方法可比性報告 — 已完成
[ ] 殘餘風險評估 — 接收方已書面簽認
[ ] 技術轉移包（TTP）— 移交完整
[ ] Outstanding Items 清單 — 責任人已指定
[ ] Lessons Learned 文件 — 已分發
[ ] 後續支援協議 — 合約已更新
[ ] 法規申請狀態 — 時間軸已確認
[ ] 知識轉移文件 — 包含隱性知識清單
[ ] 接收方回饋記錄 — 已收集並分析

重點提示：Work-Arounds 的危險性

ISPE 特別警告「work arounds（變通做法）」——那些「大家都知道但 SOP 裡沒寫」的非正式操作方式。這些通常是：

  • 短期有效但長期不可持續的解決方案
  • 新進員工不知道，老員工視為理所當然的「潛規則」
  • 若沒有納入正式程序，當關鍵人員離職時即形成知識斷層

對 CDMO 而言：在 Lessons Learned 會議後，必須系統性地將所有已知的 work-arounds 轉化為正式的 SOP 修訂，這是防止下一批次失敗的最直接行動。

實務應用：接收方的回饋如何改善未來 TT

ISPE 3.6.3.1 強調接收方必須向送出方提供回饋，且回饋時點不只在結案時，而是貫穿整個 TT 週期（包括 PPQ 期間與法規稽查期間）。對 CDMO 而言，建立系統性的回饋機制帶來兩個商業價值：

  • 內部學習：每次 TT 的 Lessons Learned 累積成 CDMO 的機構智慧，縮短下一次同類轉移的時間
  • 客戶關係：主動分享 Lessons Learned 報告（適當保密後）展現透明度，建立長期合作信任

白鴉（White Raven）等已成熟的歐洲 CDMO 之所以能縮短 TT 週期，部分原因正是他們擁有系統化的 Lessons Learned 資料庫，避免重複犯錯。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若接收方在 Phase 6 結案後發現某個 Work-Around 未被納入 SOP，但這個做法已在 PPQ 批次中使用，此時 CDMO 應如何處理？是否需要啟動偏差調查？
  2. ICH Q10 Section 1.6.1 提到知識管理的「六大來源」——請列舉這六個來源，並說明技術轉移是其中的哪個環節。
  3. 若 CDMO 在 Lessons Learned 中識別出送出方 TTP 文件品質低劣是本次 TT 延誤的主因，這個觀察如何轉化為「教訓」？具體的行動計畫應包含什麼？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • Phase 4 — 操作準備度（Operational Readiness）是技術轉移延誤的高發地帶：設備、人員、物料、程序、法規五大支柱必須全部就緒，才能啟動第一個 GMP 批次；分析方法確認應先於製程確認。
  • Engineering Runs vs. PPQ：工程試驗是非正式學習，PPQ 批次是正式 GMP 法規證據，兩者在偏差處理、批次放行和法規意涵上截然不同；PPQ 報告的六大必備要素缺一不可。
  • 分析方法可比性不只是「在規格內」，而是統計上可証明接收方的分析方法與送出方等效（精確度、準確度、系統偏差三維驗證，需統計背景人員設計）。
  • Phase 6 的轉移完成定義必須在 Charter 中事先明確——包括誰宣告完成、依據何種技術/文件/法規標準；殘餘風險必須由接收方知情書面接受。
  • 隱性知識（Tacit Knowledge）是最難轉移且最常被低估的風險：operator 的習慣操作、設備的非常規行為、有效的操作範圍——這些在 SOP 找不到，卻對生產成功至關重要。
  • CDMO 合約戰略：Phase 6 後的持續技術支援義務、法規稽查協助費率、製程更新責任，必須在合約中明確界定，避免商業糾紛。
3

Chapter 3: Analytical Method Transfer (Ch 4)

分析方法轉移 | p53-p66

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Technology Transfer (3rd Edition) | p53–p66

本章學習目標

  • 說明分析方法技術轉移的五種策略（Waiver、Co-validation、Verification、Qualitative、Quantitative Transfer Study），並辨別各自的適用條件
  • 掌握統計等效性驗收標準的意義：90% CI 雙側信賴區間、SD 與 %CV 的應用方式
  • 了解轉移前知識彙整的關鍵文件清單，包括方法開發歷史、OOS/OOT 紀錄、ATP 規格
  • 辨識技術風險評估（Technical Risk Assessment）與操作風險評估（Operational Risk Assessment）的差異與用途
  • 掌握 CDMO 作為接收方時，如何要求發送方提供完整方法歷史，以及最常見的失敗模式
4.1 Introduction — 引言

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE TT Ch.4

This chapter highlights those aspects of a technology transfer process specific to analytical methods.

The goal of an analytical method technology transfer is to ensure that knowledge from the sending unit is translated into an effective analytical method control strategy (that supports the overall product control strategy) in the receiving unit. When a receiving unit is required to perform an analytical method transfer, the company should execute an SOP to ensure:

  • Consistent practices are followed
  • Exchange of knowledge between the sending unit and the receiving unit is clear and robust
  • Data produced by the receiving unit is fit for purpose, equivalent to data from the sending unit, and defensible from both quality and regulatory standpoints

Method transfer may be required for several reasons, including:

  • Initial introduction of an analytical method into a unit that has not previously executed an equivalent method
  • Introduction into a manufacturing facility by a development group
  • Transfer from a manufacturing facility or development facility to another
  • Transfer into a third party testing unit

The level of effort, formality and documentation of the method transfer, and any testing (performed to demonstrate the success of the transfer) should be commensurate with the criticality of the respective analytical data. For example, companies may not want to spend the same amount of time on transfer specific activities for products in the early versus late stage of its lifecycle. Late stage method transfers should be rigorously performed in order to ensure success of the method transfer, in support of product release and/or inclusion of the data into regulatory registration filings.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

分析方法技術轉移 (Analytical Method Technology Transfer)：不只是「把SOP給對方」，而是確保接收方能夠產生與發送方等效、可辯護的數據。

關鍵三要素：
1. 一致性：遵循相同的 SOP 與慣例
2. 等效性：接收方數據 = 發送方數據（統計上可驗證）
3. 可辯護性：在品質與法規角度均站得住腳

比喻說明 Analogy

分析方法轉移就像「廚師換餐廳」：配方（SOP）可以帶走，但同一道菜在新廚房用不同爐具、不同水質做出來，味道可能有差。證明「一樣好吃」才是轉移成功的標準。

產品晚期（Late stage）的轉移就像米其林餐廳的招牌菜——客人（法規機構）已有期望，任何偏差都要有充分說明。

重點提示 Key Notes

風險比例原則（Commensurate with criticality）：早期臨床方法 vs. 上市前商業方法，投入的嚴謹程度截然不同。監管機構對後者的期望：完整的轉移協議、統計驗收標準、正式報告。

分析方法轉移至第三方（如 CRO 或外包實驗室）也屬於本章範疇，CDMO 業者尤其需要注意此情境。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一個 Phase I 臨床產品的 HPLC 純度方法要轉移，與 NDA 送件前的商業化轉移相比，需要的文件嚴謹程度有何差異？
  2. 「數據具有可辯護性」在 FDA 查廠時具體意味著什麼？
4.2 Technology Transfer Process — 技術轉移流程

原文內容 Original Text

4.2.1 Form an Analytical Method Transfer Team

A technology transfer team should be set up with membership from both the sending and receiving units. When the scope of the transfer includes more than one receiving unit, all impacted parties should be part of this team. This team should include the following members:

  • Sending unit's analytical method transfer coordinator and/or management with:
    • Familiarity with the development history of the analytical method
    • Experience in its operation
  • Receiving unit's analytical method transfer coordinator and/or management with:
    • Understanding of the environment in which the analytical method will be operated
    • Understanding of the constraints and capabilities that exist in that environment
  • SME from the organization that originally developed the method (e.g., the method developer) or is otherwise familiar with the development history, if available
  • Analytical and QC staff SMEs and their counterparts at the receiving unit

Additionally, consider including the QA approvers of the documents in Quality as part of the team.

Where the transfer of the analytical methods is part of a broader manufacturing process transfer, the analytical team should be a sub-team of the wider technology transfer team. An effective communication process should be established between the analytical leader(s) and the members of the wider technology transfer team.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

分析方法轉移團隊 (Analytical Method Transfer Team)：跨雙方的聯合工作小組，不是單向「發送方指導接收方」，而是雙向知識交流。

關鍵成員角色：
• 方法開發者（Method Developer / SME）：掌握方法為何如此設計，即「隱性知識」
• 接收方QC主管：最了解自家設備與環境限制
• QA代表：確保文件審批流程同步推進

比喻說明 Analogy

分析方法轉移團隊就像「建築師 + 承包商 + 建管局」的合作：建築師（方法開發者）知道設計意圖，承包商（接收方）知道在地施工條件，建管局（QA）確保合規。缺少任何一方，工程都會出問題。

重點提示 Key Notes

CDMO 常見失誤：接收方（CDMO）往往只拿到方法SOP，缺乏方法開發者的直接參與。當出現系統適用性失敗時，沒有人能解釋「為什麼當初要設這個限度」，導致調查陷入僵局。

建議：在合約階段明確要求客戶提供方法開發者聯絡窗口，並在TT協議中約定其配合義務。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若發送方的原始方法開發者已離職，CDMO 應如何處理「方法歷史知識」的空缺？
  2. 何時應將 QA 納入轉移團隊？只在簽核時才需要，還是更早期？
4.2.2 Consolidate Knowledge for the Analytical Method Transfer — 彙整分析方法知識

原文內容 Original Text

For analytical methods, key information that needs to be collated to ensure effective knowledge transfer usually includes:

  • Stage of the product lifecycle that the product is in
  • Documented history of experience with the analytical method(s) including any development and validation reports
  • Summary reports of any issues identified from data trends, analytical method deviations, and out of specification (OOS) results associated with the methods being transferred
  • Available information on the known and/or required performance criteria of the analytical method, e.g., invalid rates, acceptable uncertainty in the measurement data (Analytical Target Profile (ATP)), reporting, detection, and quantification limits
  • Documented analytical method(s) and typical chromatograms or spectra
  • Critical method controls or variables, where they have been identified
  • Analytical equipment requirements, including data handling, software versions, etc.
  • Details of analytical reference standards/reagents/columns and media
    • Where they are critical to the analytical method(s), performance details of the suppliers or grade should be shared
    • Information on availability and stability considerations, where known, should also be shared
  • Set of samples that have been selected for confirmation or comparability testing; these samples should suitably challenge the analytical method(s) and include the applicable sample matrices as appropriate
  • Summary of change controls/revisions that have been applied to the analytical method(s) since its initial validation
  • Overview of the regulatory status of the analytical method
  • HSE requirements associated with operation of the analytical method
  • Description of the importance and implications of (or contributing to) the control strategy for both drug product and drug substance

It is also important to evaluate, per method, the appropriate analytical method transfer strategy and document it appropriately.

Table 4.1: Examples of Approaches for Analytical Method Transfer
Approaches Description Points to Consider
Waiver of Method Transfer Study Can be considered for all method transfers but requires scientific justification since testing is not performed
  • The method should already be in use for a similar sample type at the receiving unit
  • The personnel at the receiving unit should have experience with the testing technique using the equivalent equipment, systems, and software
Method Co-Validation When the receiving unit participates in co-validation with the development laboratory
  • Assessment of method reproducibility between sites should be performed
  • Validation protocol should be specific to the co-validation strategy; responsibilities should be defined
Method Verification Consider for compendial methods (e.g., pH, osmolality, etc.)
  • At least one assay should be performed in the receiving unit using all appropriate sample types with appropriate success criteria (i.e., specification or historical trends) to verify performance
Qualitative Method Transfer Study For qualitative product specific methods (e.g., appearance, identity by near-infrared spectroscopy, etc.)
  • Comparative test data is usually not required; transfer is typically performed by training
  • Performed for all late/commercial stage products; could also be deemed required for clinical stage products depending on risk
Quantitative Method Transfer Study For quantitative product specific method (e.g., assay, bioassay, impurities, etc.)
  • Comparative test data is usually required
  • Performed for all late/commercial stage products; could also be deemed required for clinical stage products depending on risk

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

分析目標特性 (Analytical Target Profile, ATP)：類似產品開發中的 QTPP，ATP 定義了分析方法的預期效能上限，包括最大允許測量不確定度。是 QbD 方法開發的重要輸出文件。

OOS / OOT 歷史紀錄：這是 CDMO 最容易被忽視的要求。發送方可能會有過去的 OOS 調查紀錄或偏差報告，這些文件揭示了方法在哪些條件下容易失敗，是接收方的重要風險地圖。

重點提示 Key Notes — 五種轉移策略速查

從低風險到高複雜度：

  • Waiver（豁免）：接收方已熟悉相同技術 → 免做測試，需書面科學理由
  • Method Verification（驗證）：藥典方法（pH、滲透壓等）→ 做1次驗收測試即可
  • Qualitative Transfer（定性轉移）：外觀、NIR 鑑別等 → 以訓練為主，不需比對數據
  • Quantitative Transfer Study（定量轉移研究）：含量、雜質等 → 雙方需比對數據，有統計驗收標準
  • Co-validation（共驗證）：方法尚未完全驗證 → 雙方同步執行驗證，責任共享

比喻說明 Analogy

五種轉移策略就像餐廳「移交配方」的不同程度：
• Waiver = 廚師熟悉這道菜，只需拿SOP直接做
• Verification = 標準食譜（藥典），做一次確認口味達標
• Qualitative = 目視確認顏色外觀，訓練即可
• Quantitative = 兩家餐廳各自做一批，送第三方盲測比較
• Co-validation = 兩廚師一起研發並同時取得「星級認證」

實務應用 Practical Application — CDMO 接收方的知識要求清單

作為 CDMO，向客戶（發送方）索取以下文件才算完整：

  • 方法開發報告（Method Development Report）— 知道方法為何如此設計
  • 驗證報告（Method Validation Report）— 了解方法的效能邊界
  • OOS/OOT 歷史紀錄 — 知道方法在哪些條件下容易失敗
  • 方法修訂歷史（Change Control 紀錄）— 了解方法演變過程
  • 典型色譜圖/光譜圖 — 作為接收方的基準比較參考
  • 參考標準品資訊 — 供應商、等級、穩定性、現有庫存狀況

合約條款建議：在技術轉移協議中加入「完整方法歷史文件包」交付義務，並設定交付期限。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 客戶只提供了 SOP，沒有方法開發報告，你會如何處理？
  2. 一個 pH 方法和一個 HPLC 含量測定方法，分別最適合用哪種轉移策略？理由為何？
4.2.3 Identify Risks by Conducting Risk Assessments — 風險評估

原文內容 Original Text

For analytical method transfers, risk assessments may be divided into two types:

  • Technical risk assessments: Assessment of all high level technical risks associated with introducing the analytical method into the receiving unit. Technical risks include aspects such as analytical issues with the method, frequent failures to meet system suitability and assay acceptance, difficulties in training staff, etc.
  • Operational risk assessments: Detailed mapping exercise aimed at understanding all potential sources of variability in the operation of the analytical method and developing appropriate controls.

It may be possible to abridge risk assessments if methods, procedures, equipment, and/or equipment parameters are identical between the sending and receiving units.

4.2.3.1 Conduct a Technical Risk Assessment

The technical risk assessment should identify risks associated with utilization of the method in the new environment of the receiving unit. Table 4.2 lists questions to facilitate the risk assessment and provides suggested remediation opportunities.

Table 4.2: Technical Risk Assessment — Questions to Ask and Suggested Remediation Opportunities
Questions to Ask Suggested Remediation
Are there any known issues with the operation of the analytical method? (e.g., assay failure rates, dependencies on single source reagents, complex extractions requiring advanced training) Seek remediation to these issues from the sending unit or method developer prior to proceeding.
How well has the method performed over time? If there is a poor performing assay, ensure remediation plans are in place.
Does the receiving unit perform any methods or technologies that are similar? If the test or technology is new, seek a training plan that ensures an understanding of how the assay is performed at the sending unit.
Is the specification limit or process performance likely to be different in the receiving unit? Seek to better understand why there may be differences; put a remediation plan in place or accept these differences.
Does the receiving unit have the technology and equipment required to perform the analytical method? If the technology or equipment is new, obtain the equipment and seek training from the sending unit. Vendor training may also be beneficial.
Does the receiving unit personnel have the skills, training, and education required? Seek appropriate training from the sending unit, hire staff with prior experience, and ensure training of multiple staff to ensure redundancy.
Are there any gaps in the analytical method validation/performance information? Gaps should be addressed with the individual(s) who performed method validation.
Are there any unusual preparations or storage requirements for samples, standards, or reagents? Seek to ensure appropriate training, appropriate storage, and alignment with HSE practices.
Are controlled substances used? If so, how will they be stored? Work with the receiving unit's HSE department to put the appropriate controls in place before receipt.
Does the receiving unit understand how to obtain the sample for testing? Work with the sending unit to obtain the appropriate training and establish the appropriate procedures.
Would it benefit the receiving unit to perform a test run on a known standard to ensure readiness for transfer? Work with the sending unit to select a standard and/or sample for testing to ensure system readiness prior to starting the transfer.
Are there any critical consumables needed? (e.g., sample filters for dissolution testing to avoid API adsorption, coated HPLC vials and/or pipette tips to avoid protein binding) Work with the sending unit to identify any critical consumables needed. Obtain these consumables prior to performing the assay. If the consumable cannot be obtained, justify why an equivalent is acceptable.
Are there any special environmental requirements? (e.g., controlled humidity for inhalation products) Work with the sending unit to ensure all information related to environmental requirements are understood. Address any risks.
Is the receiving unit familiar with real time analysis technologies and model prediction? Work with the sending unit to obtain the appropriate training and establish the appropriate procedures.

The analytical method transfer may be considered low risk when:

  • For a new product with a composition that is comparable to that of an existing product and/or the concentration of active ingredient is similar to that of an existing product and is analyzed by analytical methods with which the receiving unit already has experience
  • The same as or very similar to an analytical method already in use
  • Personnel who performed the method development, method validation, or routine method analysis of a product at the sending unit are moved to the receiving unit

If the risk is considered low, a technology transfer using comparative test data may not be required.

4.2.3.2 Conduct an Operational Risk Assessment

Where the possibility exists that a receiving unit generates data that is not "right the first time" or is of a more complex nature than the receiving unit has experience, an operational risk assessment can be performed. This risk assessment is used to identify, in detail, the differences between how the analytical method is operated at the sending unit versus how it will be operated in the receiving unit.

It is good practice to use tools, such as process mapping and Ishikawa (fishbone) diagrams, to systematically identify different variables that may exist in the sending and receiving units.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

技術風險評估 (Technical Risk Assessment)：高層次，針對「方法本身」能否在新環境中運作的系統性問題清單。回答「這個方法轉過去有沒有問題？」

操作風險評估 (Operational Risk Assessment)：細節層次，針對「方法執行過程」的所有變異來源進行映射。回答「同一個方法，兩個地方做法有何不同？」

比喻說明 Analogy

技術風險評估像「搬家前的房屋勘查」：新家有沒有足夠的插座？有沒有天然氣管線？這些是搬之前就要確認的結構性問題。

操作風險評估像「搬進去後的日常試住」：發現冰箱放不進廚房、走廊燈光太暗、窗簾遮不住陽光——是執行層面的細節差異。

重點提示 Key Notes — 系統適用性：分析方法轉移的隱形陷阱

真實場景：接收方（CDMO）用了不同廠牌的 HPLC（例如 Waters vs. Agilent），雖然方法條件相同，但因為注射器死體積、梯度延遲時間、管柱溫控精度不同，導致系統適用性（System Suitability，SS）無法通過。

處理方式：

  • 提前識別儀器差異（技術風險評估問題清單第5項）
  • 在協議中預先定義「儀器等效性驗證（instrument equivalence）」步驟
  • 必要時調整SS標準（需通知客戶並記錄科學理由）
  • 極端情況：提前告知客戶需要方法修訂（method revision）再轉移

Ishikawa 魚骨圖應用 — 操作風險來源分類

分析方法操作變異來源 (6M Framework)：

Man（人員）: 操作員訓練水平、換班一致性
Machine（儀器）: HPLC型號、積分軟體版本、校正狀態
Material（物料）: 試劑批次、流動相配製水質、標準品效期
Method（方法）: SOP版本、計算公式、SS判斷標準
Measurement（量測）: 注射量、波長校正、溫度設定
Environment（環境）: 實驗室溫濕度、振動源、光照

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若接收方從未使用過生物測定法（bioassay），表格4.2中哪個問題最關鍵？應如何準備？
  2. 何種情況下可以跳過比對測試，直接用 Waiver？低風險判定三條件是什麼？
4.2.4 Readiness to Ensure Receiving Unit "Right the First Time" Execution — 接收方就緒度

原文內容 Original Text

The analytical method transfer team needs to determine the number of assays to be performed and sample types to test during training and/or readiness. Prior to performing any live transfer activities, it is recommended to perform one or more assays at the receiving unit. To evaluate unit readiness and to enable the design of readiness training and experiments, a test-a-batch exercise may be performed. This exercise is used to obtain alignment around the following requirements for the receiving unit:

  • Access to the current method
  • Access to and performed review of any supporting documentation (e.g., method validation report, method development report, control charts, etc.)
  • Appropriate equipment that are qualified as applicable
  • Appropriate software, templates, scripts, etc. that are verified and qualified
  • Appropriate materials, standards, and samples at the unit ready for use
  • Qualified staff
  • Appropriate quality systems required to support analysis in place
  • Access to any additional sample handling training for testing
  • Proficiency in similar analytical methods
  • Performed assessment of the complexity of the analytical method to be transferred
  • Performed assessment of the lifecycle state of the method (validated versus non-validated)
  • Understanding the testing that the method is for (e.g., testing for stability indicating methods depend on the degradation pathway)
  • Predetermination of the number of readiness assays that may be completed at the receiving unit if training occurs at the sending unit

If readiness results are determined to be unacceptable, a plan should be developed to assess the root cause including, but not limited to, training, method performance, equipment, materials/samples, and calculations.

Depending on the complexity of each analytical method, it may be useful for representatives from the receiving unit to directly observe the operation of analytical methods at the sending unit in order to ensure effective transfer of all tactical knowledge. Additionally, it may be useful for the sending unit team to observe the receiving unit in order to build a good understanding of the equipment and establish capability at a practical level.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Test-a-Batch Exercise（試批演練）：在正式轉移協議執行前，接收方以真實樣品或模擬樣品進行一次或多次「預熱運行」，目的是確認就緒度而非產生用於接收的數據。

「Right the First Time」原則：正式轉移協議的數據應該是「一次到位」，不是反覆試錯。這需要充分的前期準備，而非直接衝進協議執行。

比喻說明 Analogy

就緒度評估就像「彩排（Dress Rehearsal）」：正式演出（轉移協議執行）前，先做一場完整彩排。彩排暴露的問題可以在不影響正式紀錄的情況下修正。

接收方到發送方觀摩 = 演員到原版劇組觀摩學習「隱性表演技巧」；發送方到接收方視察 = 導演到新場地確認舞台設備。

重點提示 Key Notes

就緒度核查清單的實務重點（CDMO 角度）：

  • 設備資格（Equipment Qualification）：儀器必須有效的校正與 IQ/OQ/PQ 紀錄才能用於 GMP 測試
  • 軟體版本：色譜數據系統（CDS）版本需與方法SOP相容，不同版本的積分算法可能造成系統性差異
  • 穩定性指示方法（Stability Indicating Method）：需要準備含有對應降解物的樣品來驗證降解分離能力，不能只用新鮮樣品

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若就緒度測試結果不合格，根本原因調查應從哪五個方向切入？
  2. 接收方人員親赴發送方觀摩的主要目的是什麼？哪類方法最有必要安排這樣的交流？
4.2.5–4.2.6 Analytical Method Transfer Plan and Protocol — 轉移計畫與協議

原文內容 Original Text

4.2.5 Analytical Method Transfer Plan

An analytical method transfer plan, with a project plan to evaluate timing and resources, is recommended for the transfer of two or more methods. The implementation strategy should account for the following factors:

  • Experience and knowledge of the receiving unit
  • Degree of familiarity of the receiving unit with the methodology or technology used
  • Specification of the product
  • Complexity of the analytical method

The method transfer plan should include details of how many repetitions will be performed and how the performance of the analytical method will be assessed. The number of repetitions should be adequate to provide sufficient statistical confidence.

At this stage, it may be useful to define the maximum acceptable uncertainty in the data (as per the ATP, if available). This can be established by setting equivalency criteria using a specific statistical test for demonstrating comparability between units. It requires that the two-sided 90% confidence interval (or two, one-sided 95% confidence bounds) for the difference in units fits entirely inside pre-established bounds.

Table 4.3: Suggested Contents for Analytical Method Transfer Plan
Section Number Section Title
1Purpose
2Roles and Responsibilities
3References
4Analytical Method Training
5Analytical Method Transfer Strategy
6Analytical Method Validation Strategy (as required)
7Qualification of Reference Standards
8Assessment of Critical Reagents
9Analytical Method Validation History
10Sample Testing Matrix

4.2.6 Analytical Method Transfer Protocol

An analytical method transfer protocol should be generated to address each method being transferred. The cumulative knowledge available should be used to establish a transfer protocol that ensures appropriate experiments are performed to demonstrate that the analytical method produces data in the receiving unit which are fit for purpose.

The criteria should include a description of any statistical methods to be used in analyzing collected data and any provision for addressing deviations from expected conditions and handling of nonconforming data. Data should not be excluded from further consideration without a documented, science-based justification.

For each test involved in the transfer, the type of transfer should be clearly articulated. Transfer types may comprise:

  • Paper exercise/scientific justification, i.e. waiver
  • Method verification
  • Local validation of particular aspects of the method
  • Full side by side comparison of data generated on the appropriate sample by each of the sending and receiving units

The transfer protocol needs to contain predetermined success criteria and be approved prior to execution.

Further recommendations for the analytical method transfer protocol include:

  • Engaging support from the method developer and statisticians to set the study design and success criteria
  • Using historical data to fulfill the success criteria if justified in the protocol versus performing comparative testing
  • Selecting sample types that are representative of the materials being tested at the receiving unit:
    • Consider lots of the same formulation, different formulations/strengths, and different sample types
    • Use the reference standard or assay control as one of the samples for bias assessment
    • For stability indicating methods, include a stability sample, preferably one with a relevant level of degradation
    • For products with multiple strengths, bracketing may be appropriate
    • For qualitative assays, include a negative control sample where possible
    • Set aside ample retain samples in all instances
    • Consider the impact of any shipments of samples between units
  • Justifying the use of any alternate equipment or reagents at the receiving unit
  • If a method revision is required prior to the approval of the protocol, providing a draft of the method along with the protocol for approval
  • Including both the receiving and sending units in protocol review and/or approval
"The samples selected for confirmation or comparability testing should suitably challenge the analytical method. For example, it is recommended to utilize samples with impurity levels close to acceptance and/or threshold criteria in order to evaluate the receiving unit's ability to reach the same quality decisions as the sending unit."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

轉移計畫 (Transfer Plan) vs. 轉移協議 (Transfer Protocol) 的差異：

• 計畫（Plan）：整體藍圖，涵蓋所有方法、策略選擇、資源與時程安排，可跨多個方法

• 協議（Protocol）：個別方法的詳細實驗設計，包含具體驗收標準、統計方法與樣品清單，需要事先批准

類比：計畫是「建案規劃書」，協議是「每棟建築的施工圖」。

統計等效性標準 Statistical Equivalence Criteria

等效性測試（Two One-Sided Tests, TOST）：

判定標準：
接收方均值與發送方均值之差的
90% 雙側信賴區間必須完全落在
預設邊界（equivalence bounds）之內

範例（HPLC 含量測定）：
等效邊界設定：± 2.0%（絕對值）
實測 90% CI：[-0.8%, +1.2%]
→ 完全落在邊界內 → 通過等效性

若 CI 超出邊界（例如 [-0.8%, +2.5%]）
→ 等效性不成立 → 需調查

常用指標：
• Mean difference（均值差）
• 90% CI for difference
• SD / %CV（中間精確度）
• %RSD（重現性）

重點提示 Key Notes — 預定驗收標準的重要性

必須「事先」定義驗收標準，不能「事後」調整：這是監管機構最關注的數據完整性議題。若在看到數據後才更改標準，即使有合理理由，都可能引發數據可靠性質疑。

數據排除規則：無效分析（Invalid Assay）的排除需有事先定義在協議中的準則，加上事後的書面科學理由，二者缺一不可。

樣品選擇的挑戰性原則：應選擇含有接近規格上限雜質的樣品（stressed sample），而非「最乾淨」的樣品。這才能真實評估接收方的分辨能力。

比喻說明 Analogy

預定驗收標準就像考試的評分標準：必須在考試前公布，不能在看完學生的答案後才決定60分還是70分算及格。否則就是「看數據調標準」，與學術不端行為無異。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼穩定性指示方法（stability indicating method）的轉移需要包含有降解物的樣品？若用新鮮樣品測試有什麼風險？
  2. 客戶的含量方法轉移協議沒有統計等效性標準，只有「結果需在標示量 95–105%」。這樣的標準有什麼問題？
4.2.7–4.2.8 Execute and Report the Analytical Method Transfer — 執行與報告

原文內容 Original Text

4.2.7 Execute the Analytical Method Transfer

The receiving unit staff performs the transfer or qualification experiments as outlined in the analytical method transfer protocol. Data review and assessment of the results should be performed with the sending unit staff, preferably as the method transfer is being executed to prevent any delays in understanding issues with the data being generated throughout protocol execution. The sending unit should be notified of any invalid assays and unexpected results.

Care should be taken to ensure that the integrity of the samples is unaffected by the shipping process between units.

The transfer protocol should define which reference standards are to be used in any testing and from where they are to be obtained.

The defined local operating instructions should be followed during execution of the transfer protocol. The transfer exercise should be performed under normal conditions by the personnel routinely expected to perform the analytical method. Any testing performed during the execution of the transfer should be performed by operators that have been fully trained in all relevant aspects of the required techniques.

A review of the transfer should be performed by the sending unit and the receiving unit. Questions to consider during the review include:

  • Is the data being produced in the receiving unit considered fit for purpose?
  • Is the analytical method operating reliably in the receiving unit?
  • Are there any improvements to the analytical method to consider?

4.2.8 Analytical Method Transfer Report

The receiving unit should generate a report outlining the pre-approved protocol success criteria and an assessment against the criteria for each of the analytical methods involved in the transfer.

If the success criteria are not met, it is important to follow the receiving unit's quality system to investigate. Consideration should be given to such aspects as training, equipment, reagents, environmental conditions, success criteria (i.e., not set correctly), etc. to determine the root cause. All exceptional conditions outside of the pre-approved protocol should be documented and justified, including all invalid assays.

If an analytical method transfer is unsuccessful, an investigation should be performed per the appropriate QMS and next steps should be determined.

Table 4.5: Example Analytical Method Transfer Report with Protocol Success Criteria and Results
Performance Characteristic Sample Type Success Criteria Results Met / Not Met
Equivalency Reference Standard The bounds of the 90% CI for the difference in the receiving unit mean from the historical mean must fall entirely within:
% Attribute 1: ± 0.95%
% Attribute 2: ± 0.92%		 90% CI for the difference:
% Attribute 1: [-0.019, +0.58]
% Attribute 2: [-0.60, -0.00055]		 Met
Intermediate Precision Assay Control The intermediate precision (SD) for the n determinations obtained in the receiving unit must be:
SD ≤ 2 for both Attribute 1 and Attribute 2		 Attribute 1 %CV = 2.2% (SD = 0.7)
Attribute 2 %CV = 1.2% (SD = 0.7)		 Met
Reproducibility Assay Control The assay control for each determination must not be more than 2.0% RSD 2.4% RSD Not Met

Note: CI, Confidence Interval; CV, Coefficient of Variation; RSD, Relative Standard Deviation; SD, Standard Deviation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

同步數據審閱（Real-time data review）：不等到協議全部完成才給發送方看數據——而是執行過程中持續分享。這樣可以即時發現問題，避免整批數據失敗後才調查。

轉移報告的核心結構：預設標準（from Protocol）→ 實際結果（from experiments）→ 判定（Met/Not Met）→ 調查（if Not Met）。格式如 Table 4.5 所示。

重點提示 Key Notes — 解讀 Table 4.5 的「Not Met」

重現性（Reproducibility）結果 2.4% RSD，超過 2.0% 標準 → 不合格。

此時的正確流程：

  • 不能自行調整標準或排除數據
  • 開立偏差調查（Deviation Investigation）
  • 分析根本原因（操作員一致性？儀器穩定性？樣品均勻性？）
  • 決定後續行動：重跑測試、方法修訂或接受風險評估
  • 正式結案後才能宣告轉移成功或失敗

注意：2.4% vs. 2.0% 的差距雖然只有 0.4%，但如果事前沒有科學理由，就是「不合格」，不是「差不多」。

比喻說明 Analogy

轉移報告就像「新員工試用期評估表」：每個 KPI 都有事先設定的達標標準，試用期結束後逐條對照。有一項未達標不代表全部失敗，但必須啟動改善計畫，不能假裝沒看見。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 分析方法轉移最常見的失敗模式：

  • 第一名：文件不完整 — 客戶只給 SOP，沒有驗證報告和方法開發歷史，導致轉移中出現問題時無法追溯根本原因
  • 第二名：標準品問題 — 轉移完成後客戶的原級標準品（Primary RS）用盡且停產，CDMO 無法繼續使用相同標準品體系
  • 第三名：系統適用性失敗 — 雙方 HPLC 型號不同，方法沒有預先做儀器等效性評估

預防策略：在合約談判階段就明確文件交付清單、標準品供應計畫、儀器規格要求，而非等到執行阶段才發現問題。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. Table 4.5 中，重現性未達標但前兩項達標，你作為接收方 QC 主管，下一步應該做什麼？
  2. 轉移執行期間，接收方發現有一次分析（assay）結果異常高，應如何處理？可以直接排除嗎？
4.3 Points to Consider — 注意事項

原文內容 Original Text

4.3.1 Site Selection

The receiving unit should be included in any site selection process when it comes to technology transfers. Typically, focus is placed on the manufacturing area; however, capital equipment and instrument costs can be high in the QC space as well as expense costs for training, travel, consumables, etc. These costs should be considered up front to ensure that the overall technology transfer budget will be met.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

場地選擇中的分析成本：技術轉移的成本分析往往聚焦在製造端（設備採購、廠房改造），但 QC 分析端的成本也可能非常可觀：高效液相色譜儀、質譜儀、生物測定設備等，單台儀器費用就可達數百萬元。

重點提示 Key Notes

CDMO 報價中常被低估的分析成本：

  • 新儀器採購與 IQ/OQ/PQ 費用
  • 員工訓練與出差費用（到發送方觀摩）
  • 參考標準品與關鍵試劑的首批採購
  • 方法開發或再驗證的潛在費用（若方法需調整）
  • 初期較高的分析失敗率（方法熟悉期的額外消耗）

建議在商務談判早期就進行分析方法清單盤點，避免後期追加費用引發客戶不滿。

比喻說明 Analogy

QC 分析成本就像搬家時的「隱形費用」：大家都在算搬家車費（製造端），卻忘了新家要安裝的窗簾、電燈、網路、重新辦理的各種繳費帳號（QC 儀器和試劑）。最後才發現「怎麼超預算這麼多？」

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若客戶的方法需要用到特殊生物測定設備，而 CDMO 目前沒有，是否應該承接這個 TT 案？應如何評估？
  2. 在 TT 協議談判中，哪些 QC 相關費用應由發送方負擔，哪些由接收方自行吸收？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • 五種分析方法轉移策略：Waiver（豁免）→ Verification（驗證）→ Qualitative Study（定性研究）→ Quantitative Study（定量研究）→ Co-validation（共驗證），依風險與方法類型選擇
  • 統計等效性：以 90% 雙側信賴區間（Two One-Sided Tests, TOST）判定，CI 必須完全落在預設邊界內，事前定義、不可事後更改
  • 風險評估雙軌：Technical（高層技術風險）和 Operational（執行操作差異）兩種評估互補，缺一不可
  • 預定驗收標準先行：協議必須在執行前批准，數據排除必須有書面科學理由，無效分析必須全部記錄
  • CDMO 最常見失敗模式：方法歷史文件不完整 → 在合約階段就要求「完整方法開發文件包」的交付義務
  • 系統適用性陷阱：不同 HPLC 型號可能導致 SS 失敗，技術風險評估中應提前識別並規劃儀器等效性評估
  • QC 成本被低估：場地選擇時應同步評估分析端的資本支出與運營費用，納入 TT 整體預算
4

Chapter 4: Drug Substance Transfer (Ch 5)

原料藥技術轉移 | p67-p82

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Technology Transfer (3rd Edition) | p67–p82

本章學習目標

  • 區分小分子 API (Active Pharmaceutical Ingredient，活性藥物成分) 與大分子生物製劑在技術轉移上的核心差異，理解為何兩者需要不同的可比性策略
  • 掌握技術轉移套件 (Technology Transfer Package) 的完整架構：製程資訊、物料資訊、分析方法、廠房設備規格四大類別
  • 理解風險/可行性評估的目的與方法，學習如何利用差距分析 (Gap Analysis) 識別製程知識缺口與設備改造需求
  • 了解工程批次、PPQ 批次的執行邏輯，以及轉移成功標準的評估方式
  • 具備接受 DS 技術轉移的 CDMO 就緒性檢核思維：設備等效性、分析平台、原料供應商管理、法規歷史
5.1 Introduction — 導論

原文內容 Original Text ISPE TechTransfer Ch.5

This chapter provides specific guidance for technology transfer of drug substance processes for large molecules (e.g., recombinant proteins, monoclonal antibodies) or small synthetic molecules. This guidance is intended to be relevant to all technology transfers between sending and receiving units.

For this reason, some aspects included in this chapter may not be applicable to specific transfer programs that are usually dependent on the stage in the product lifecycle. For example, early stage transfers (from one R&D group to another), transfers of supporting laboratory scale processes, and transfers of limited process scope may not require all the elements presented.

Technology transfer teams should review the guidance provided and determine which are appropriate for their situation. This chapter can be read as a stand-alone guide for drug substance technology transfer. Further relevant information is included in the complete Guide; references to other chapters in the Guide are therefore included.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 小分子 vs. 大分子 DS

小分子 API (Small Molecule API)：化學合成定義明確的化合物，分子量小，結構可完整表徵。可比性較易建立，主要透過 ICH Q3A 雜質控制與 ICH Q6A 規格確認。

大分子生物藥 (Large Molecule / Biologic)：包括重組蛋白、單株抗體 (mAb)。分子量大、結構複雜，生物活性受製程條件（細胞株、上游/下游製程）深度影響。可比性需廣泛分析與功能性表徵，依據 ICH Q5E。

核心差異：小分子的「化學等同」較易判定；大分子的「生物等效」必須透過多層次測試才能確認。

比喻說明

小分子 API 技術轉移就像把一道有固定食譜的料理搬到新廚房——換了爐子和炒鍋，食材不變，只要確認火候和比例正確，成品幾乎相同。大分子生物藥的轉移則像移植一座活的酒莊——光是複製設備不夠，葡萄藤（細胞株）、土壤（培養基）、氣候（環境條件）都會影響最終的酒體風味（蛋白質摺疊與糖基化）。

重點提示

本章明確指出：並非所有元素都適用於每次轉移。早期臨床轉移、實驗室規模轉移的要求低於商業規模轉移。團隊必須根據產品生命週期階段決定哪些步驟是必要的，避免過度設計導致進度延誤。

練習思考

  1. 一個 CDMO 同時承接小分子 API 與 mAb 的技術轉移，哪一個需要更多的分析可比性工作？原因為何？
  2. 早期臨床階段的轉移與商業化轉移，在技術轉移套件的完整性要求上有何不同？
5.2 Technology Transfer Process — 技術轉移流程

原文內容 Original Text

The focus of this chapter is on the product and process specific requirements of the technology transfer (from the initial high level technology transfer proposal to operational readiness and process/procedure qualification) as analytical method requirements are covered in Chapter 4. Where relevant, aspects that are specific to only large molecule or small molecule drug substance will be indicated.

Information on forming a technology transfer team and developing a charter is presented within Chapters 2 and 3.

5.2.1 Initial Risk/Feasibility Assessment

An initial risk assessment will be required to determine whether the technology transfer of the process and product to the receiving unit is feasible (see also Section 2.2). Prior to obtaining a detailed technology transfer package from the sending unit, sufficient information to perform an initial, high level assessment of the process at the receiving unit should be obtained. At this stage, especially if the process is being transferred to an external company, it may not be possible to share very much information due to confidentiality restrictions and documents may be redacted.

During this feasibility assessment, a skeleton cross-functional team at the potential receiving unit (representing process, analytical, operations, HSE, materials management, regulatory, and quality) should perform an initial risk assessment based on the targeted markets and desired volumes against the product specification, mass balance, raw materials, and the block/process flow diagram.

For example, potential safety hazards, toxicity of the materials, corrosive nature, unique analytical requirements, raw material supply, and plant capacity are factors that should be assessed as part of this early stage risk assessment.

The rationale for evaluating product specification, mass balance, raw materials, and block/process flow diagram in the initial risk assessment are as follows:

  • Depending on the stage in the product lifecycle, the regulatory strategy required to meet the business strategy should be part of the initial focus of the technology transfer. If a product specification has been filed at the sending unit, this will form the basis of the technology transfer to ensure the product at the receiving unit meets the targeted market requirements, with justification of differences from existing pharmacopoeia requirements. The CQAs in the product specification are not the only items needing to be successfully produced as other quality attributes may be difficult to achieve in a new manufacturing facility.
  • A mass balance defines the plant capacity highlighting where equipment changes may be required. For large molecules, equipment changes are likely to be required if the product titer is low at harvest and the drug substance final product concentration is high. For small molecule API manufacture, the mass balance serves to provide process stream composition based on both analytical data and computational analysis. Balanced chemical equations identifying all side- and by-products of the process chemistry need to be part of the initial risk assessment.
  • Assessment of the raw materials establishes critical supply chain, analytical complexity, and any safety constraints.
  • The block/process flow diagram provides an overview of the process defined at the sending unit to gain better understanding of the plant requirements.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 初步風險/可行性評估的四大維度

  • 產品規格 (Product Specification)：已申報的規格就是轉移的底線。接收單位必須確認能達到相同或等效的 CQA 水準，差異需要有科學依據說明。
  • 質量平衡 (Mass Balance)：大分子決定設備規模（例如低效價原液需要更大的純化柱）；小分子則揭示副反應產物與廢棄物流。
  • 原料 (Raw Materials)：供應商認可、分析複雜度、安全限制（如 ICH M7 基因毒性雜質）。
  • 製程流程圖 (BFD/PFD)：讓接收單位在拿到完整資料前先理解製程全貌。

比喻說明 — 評估前的 due diligence

初步可行性評估就像買房前的房屋鑑定——不需要拆開每一面牆，但要確認基礎結構、電路容量、地基是否能承載你的需求。CDMO 接收評估也一樣：在簽約前先確認廠房、設備、分析能力是否能「承載」這個製程。

重點提示 — 保密協定 (NDA/CDA) 的現實限制

初始評估階段，送出單位往往因保密限制只能提供有限資訊（甚至需要遮蓋關鍵部分）。這正是為什麼 BFD 和質量平衡如此重要——它們是在不揭露完整製程細節的情況下仍能進行評估的最小資訊集。CDMO 業務開發團隊應建立標準化的「接收可行性評估問卷」，明確列出最低需求資訊清單。

實務應用 — CDMO 接收就緒性清單（初步評估）

  • 廠房是否有符合製程規模的生物反應器 / 反應釜？
  • 是否具備相關 API 的處理資質（如高活性化合物、生物製品）？
  • 分析平台是否支援所需的測試項目（HPLC、生物活性測試、細胞活性試驗）？
  • 現有原料供應商名單是否覆蓋關鍵起始物料？
  • 法規歷史（藥政審查記錄）是否符合目標市場要求？

練習思考

  1. 一個大分子產品的收穫效價 (harvest titer) 只有 0.5 g/L，但目標原液濃度是 20 mg/mL。這對接收廠房的設備規格意味著什麼？
  2. 為何 CQA 不是唯一的轉移標準？舉例說明在新廠難以複製的非 CQA 品質屬性。
5.2.2 Consolidate Knowledge for Technology Transfer Package — 整合知識形成技術轉移套件

原文內容 Original Text

Once the initial risk assessment has been performed and the receiving unit has been identified, the formal technology transfer can proceed. Confidentiality agreements may be required before the technology transfer package can be sent to an external company. A structured approach to sharing process and product information should be agreed upon upfront. Use of a controlled/defined file sharing system helps to limit large email traffic and allows for secure transfer of information and organization of information type (e.g., development reports, batch records, analytical information) between the sending and receiving units.

A checklist of information/documents for large and small molecule processes is provided in Chapter 8 (Appendix 1).

5.2.2.1 Process Information

  • Block Flow Diagrams (BFDs) are a Lean tool used to improve processes. For technology transfers, they ensure that the process steps are understood, in the correct order, and identify all process streams including waste and by-products. They can also serve the same function as the Process Flow Diagram and since they are typically easier to develop, can be used to quickly compare processing options. An example BFD is shown in Figure 5.1.
  • Process Flow Diagrams (PFDs) aid visualization of key data, e.g., processing times, in-process testing, etc. PFDs from all previous installations of the process (different sites or scales) can be helpful, especially for supporting updates to regulatory filings.
  • Process overview descriptions written in a site and scale-independent way so that the particulars of the existing implementation(s) are not confused with the generic requirements or validated ranges. Examples include: tabular data for process setpoints, acceptable ranges for unit operations as well as media and buffer preparations, descriptions of operating procedures and strategies, critical and other important process parameters, CQAs, and KPIs.
  • Manufacturing batch records (blank and/or examples of executed documents where relevant) can be the starting point for the receiving unit to generate their internal batch records.
  • SOPs from the sending unit provide information about detailed operation procedures (e.g., particle sizing for small molecules), although these may be related to site specific equipment and procedures.
  • Drug substance/process control strategy and the link between drug product CQAs, CPPs, potential CPPs, and drug substance manufacturing requirements.
  • CPV data generated to support process parameter trending and any statistical process control analysis.
  • Process observation for transfer of the often tacit process knowledge that arises from hands-on operating experience — e.g., addition of component #4 always causes a color change, pictures of typical cell morphology.
  • PAT (Process Analytical Technology), as relevant.
  • Storage and shipping conditions for final drug substance, including container type, packaging requirements, and any specific transportation requirements or validation.
  • Process intermediate and final drug substance stability information to identify stability constraints that affect hold times between steps or timing of product release for shipping.
  • Process specific deviations, investigations, and CAPAs from GMP batches.
  • Extractables/leachables/elemental impurities knowledge and to clarify which disposable equipment is suitable for use in the process.
  • Spreadsheet-based process models to facilitate process fit at the receiving unit — e.g., predicting column sizes depending on a range of harvest titers.
  • Product and reagent safety documentation detailing any potency concerns and cleanability issues.

Historical data is valuable for product comparability and includes: historical process manufacturing reports, historical process and analytical data (SPC trend charts, tabulated means/ranges), process development reports, virus clearance data (for mammalian-origin molecules), small scale model qualification, process characterization reports (DoE studies, design space, CPPs, Proven Acceptable Ranges), process validation reports, reports from prior transfers, annual product reviews, regulatory license documents, and change control summaries.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 技術轉移套件的四大類資料

完整的技術轉移套件包含四個層次，由粗到細：

  • 製程資訊 (Process Information)：BFD、PFD、批次記錄、SOP、控制策略、CPV 數據
  • 物料資訊 (Materials Information)：原料規格、細胞庫（大分子）、供應商清單
  • 分析方法資訊 (Analytical Method Information)：藥典法、in-house 方法、驗證報告
  • 廠房設備資訊 (Facility/Equipment Information)：P&ID、URS/FRS、自動化控制需求、清潔驗證

比喻說明 — 默會知識的轉移

文字 SOP 傳遞的是「顯性知識」，就像樂譜；真正讓音樂活起來的是演奏家的「默會知識 (tacit knowledge)」——手腕的力道、呼吸的節奏。製程觀察 (Process Observation) 和 SME 駐廠支援，就是讓接收單位的操作員親眼看到「加入第四種原料時液體會變色」這類無法寫進 SOP 的經驗。這也是為什麼現場學習比閱讀文件更有價值。

重點提示 — BFD vs. PFD 的功能差異

BFD (Block Flow Diagram，方塊流程圖)：快速、高層次，適合早期評估和跨廠比較。重點是製程步驟順序、物料流和廢棄物流。

PFD (Process Flow Diagram，製程流程圖)：詳細的工程圖，包含處理時間、在製程測試點、設備容積等數據。適合後續工程評估與法規申報更新。

兩者皆需要，不可相互替代。

關鍵資料類型速覽

技術轉移套件層次 (由粗至細)：
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Level 1 — 製程總覽                       │
│  BFD → PFD → 製程描述 → setpoint 表格    │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Level 2 — 執行層文件                     │
│  批次記錄 → SOP → 控制策略表             │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Level 3 — 歷史數據                       │
│  CPV 數據 → 製程表徵報告 → 驗證報告      │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ Level 4 — 支援性資訊                     │
│  偏差/CAPA → E&L → 安全文件 → 穩定性     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘

練習思考

  1. 為什麼製程描述應以「與廠址和規模無關 (site and scale-independent)」的方式撰寫？若不這樣做，接收單位會遇到什麼問題？
  2. 病毒清除數據 (Virus Clearance Data) 為何只在哺乳動物來源的大分子中才需要？
5.2.2.2–5.2.2.4 Materials, Analytical & Facility Information — 物料、分析方法與廠房設備資訊

原文內容 Original Text

5.2.2.2 Materials Information

Early alignment of raw materials or consumables used in the process will facilitate transfer. Materials information include:

  • Specifications of raw materials
  • Critical material attributes
  • CQAs for raw materials that can impact the final API (for small molecules)
  • Bill of materials for the process
  • Media and buffer formulations, including titrants used for pH adjustments
  • Other materials/consumables (e.g., filters, bags, gaskets/O-rings, tubing, sieves for sifters, screens for milling) — including lead times
  • Identification of new materials such as disposables/consumables and understanding of lead times (see Table 5.4)
  • Current suppliers and catalog numbers — primary and secondary sources, including audit findings
  • Identification of acceptable alternative materials (see Table 5.5)
  • Identification of receiving unit restrictions on suppliers or materials
  • Cell bank, origin of cell bank, cell bank testing (large molecule only)
  • Appropriate general safety documentation
  • Excipient risk assessments
Table 5.4: Example Comparison of Materials between Sending and Receiving Units
Component Specified by Sending Unit Closest Equivalent at Receiving Unit Comments
Millipak® 20 (0.2 μm) filter Millipak® 60 (0.2 μm) filter Equivalent acceptable
Supplier A depth filter for harvest Supplier B depth filter for harvest Equivalent acceptable
Sartopore® 2 (0.2 μm + 0.1 μm) filter Pall Fluorodyne Kleenpak® (0.1μm) filter Equivalent acceptable, same membrane type
1 L and 500 ml Teflon® bottles for drug substance bulk fill High-density polyethylene Nalgenes® for drug substance bulk fill Teflon® bottles to be sourced
Sodium phosphate dihydrate Sodium phosphate monohydrate and heptahydrate available Buffers to be reformulated and evaluated at small scale
L-Histidine base Multi-compendial grade routinely sourced from supplier 1 Process specific requirement from new supplier required

5.2.2.3 Analytical Method Information

To support in-process and drug substance testing at the receiving unit, early establishment of analytical methods is a critical activity (see Chapter 4). At a minimum, the following information is required:

  • Compendial (e.g., USP) or other qualified methods used for all raw materials and final drug substance
  • In-house methods used for all raw materials and final drug substance
  • Method qualification and validation protocols/reports at sending unit
  • In-process sample control specifications and methods
  • Setup and qualification of raw material and reagent testing at the receiving unit — this can be a long lead item

5.2.2.4 Facility/Equipment Specifications and Capabilities Information

Information on specific process details that affect the facility/equipment for the manufacturing process should be highlighted early on in the technology transfer to allow any facility modifications at the receiving unit to be priced out, planned, and implemented. This information includes:

  • Piping and Instrumentation Diagrams (P&IDs) for equipment that may be specific to the process
  • Equipment User Requirements Specification (URS) and/or Functional Requirements Specification (FRS)
  • Automation/process control requirements (e.g., pH control strategy, nutrient feed control strategy, controlled rate freezing, UF/DF, chromatography)
  • System size and capacity — suitability of available vessels, piping diameters, pumps, etc.
  • Capability for temperature control if needed
  • Requirements for particular sensors or analytical equipment where differences in types (sensitivity, methodology) or suppliers may result in skewed measurements
  • Cleaning procedures, development studies, validation reports
  • Safety assessments and/or information on hazardous waste or other waste streams specific to the process
  • Instrumentation requirements (pH meters, control systems, PAT technology used, etc.)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 細胞庫轉移 (Cell Bank Transfer) — 大分子獨有挑戰

大分子的製程核心是「細胞株 (Cell Line)」。轉移時必須同步轉移：

  • 主細胞庫 (Master Cell Bank, MCB)：WHO/ICH Q5B 要求完整的表徵套件（身份、純度、穩定性）隨技術轉移一併提交
  • 工作細胞庫 (Working Cell Bank, WCB)：接收單位可能需要建立自己的 WCB，需要再次表徵
  • 法規複雜性：細胞庫轉移本身可能觸發 CMC 申報更新，需要提前與監管機構溝通策略

這是大分子轉移時間線最容易被低估的環節之一。

重點提示 — 等效物料的評估原則

Table 5.4 的例子顯示真實轉移中的物料替換決策。評估原則：

  • 過濾器：相同膜孔徑、相同膜材料 → 可接受等效
  • 緩衝液鹽類水合物差異：需在小規模重新評估配方（pH、滲透壓）
  • 容器材料（Teflon vs. HDPE）：需要 E&L 相容性評估

原則：「等效可接受」需有科學依據文件，不能僅憑外觀相似就判定。

比喻說明 — 分析方法是「翻譯器」

分析方法就像兩個廠房之間的「翻譯器」——同一個製程，用不同廠商的 HPLC 測出的數字可能有系統性偏差 (bias)。如果翻譯器不準確，即使製程做得完全一樣，數據對話也會「雞同鴨講」。這就是為什麼分析方法的轉移需要在 PPQ 批次之前完成——因為你需要確定數據是可信的才能做比較。

廠房設備評估框架

設備等效性評估矩陣：
┌───────────────┬──────────────┬────────────┐
│ 設備項目       │ 送出單位規格  │ 接收單位狀態│
├───────────────┼──────────────┼────────────┤
│ 生物反應器容積 │ 2000 L       │ 1500 L (差距)│
│ 色層管柱直徑   │ 60 cm        │ 45 cm (需評估)│
│ UF/DF 膜面積  │ 50 m²        │ 35 m²       │
│ pH 控制系統    │ Mettler-T.   │ Endress+H.  │
└───────────────┴──────────────┴────────────┘
每個差距 → 需要風險評估 + 緩解計畫

練習思考

  1. 為什麼 P&ID 和 URS 需要在技術轉移早期就提供，而不是等到工程批次前才交出？
  2. 「原料測試的資格確認是長交期項目 (long lead item)」——請解釋這句話的實際含義，並說明如何在時間線規劃中處理。
5.2.3 Technology Transfer Operational Readiness — 技術轉移作業就緒

原文內容 Original Text

Gap Analysis / Risk Mitigation

Once the technology transfer package has been obtained, the receiving unit can then initiate a process gap analysis in order to compare how the process was operated at the sending unit to how the process will be operated at the receiving unit. This will identify:

  • Where there are gaps in process knowledge
  • Where process changes may be required to fit the new facility
  • Whether any engineering modifications are required for the new facility

Section 3.3.2 describes approaches to risk analysis and evaluation and the tools that can be used. By considering the severity (impact), occurrence (probability) and detection, a risk priority number (RPN) can be derived. This can be used as a basis for determining the level of risk and whether mitigations are required. Examples of process gap analyses are provided in Section 5.4. The gap analysis is often the first opportunity for the transfer team to intensively review the process together, and thus can serve as a good learning exercise for the receiving unit.

Transfer and Implementation of Laboratory Scale Process

If possible, the laboratory scale version of the process should be transferred prior to (or concurrently with) the full scale process transfer. This provides the receiving technical unit the opportunity to work with the process hands-on and catch any details that may have been overlooked in the technology transfer package.
